World Trade Stagnation 72

A Few Countries Pursuing Self-Interest Causing the Current Situation

The United States Suffers Greater Losses Than Other Countries

Report by the League of Nations Economic Investigation Group

(Geneva) After a detailed examination of world market trade from 1929 to 1933, the League of Nations Economic Investigation Group learned that the stagnation of world trade is like a [beast] occupying it, and now the spine of this beast must be broken, but it has not yet reached its death. According to the group's investigation, the trade situation in 1933 did show signs of gradual recovery, but its progress was inevitably somewhat slow. Furthermore, upon examination of the trade movements of all parties in 1933, although competition was fierce, price changes were still unpredictable. A few countries have tried their best to seek the revival of their own business, but they are only seeking it for themselves, which does not help the stagnation of the world. The reason for this is that the failure to restore international market credit and the failure to achieve stable exchange rates are all the sources of the disease. The inability to move gold reserves and the excessively strict exchange restrictions are sufficient to hinder price balance. According to most observers, the investigation group's report is not enough to save the stagnant phenomenon of world trade. It is faintly heard that the United States may initiate the reopening of the [failed London Economic Conference]. The investigation group once said that the trade of goods exchanged between countries in the world has fallen by more than 30% compared with previous years. If calculated using gold as a standard, the total value of goods exchanged between countries in 1933 was only more than 50% of that in 1929. If the quantity and value of goods are mixed for calculation, it is only half of that in 1929. As world trade has suffered such a terrible decline, international debts cannot be paid as scheduled. According to a statistician in the League of Nations who used gold as the standard to count the losses suffered by the United States in trade in 1933, it was actually greater than that of other countries. Therefore, although it is gratifying that world trade is slightly recovering, in fact, if no urgent rescue measures are taken to reverse the dangerous situation of this stagnation, the future is still difficult to be optimistic. (4th, National Telegraph)

British Finances Sound 74

The United States Pales in Comparison

(London) The UK's budget position is very good, unlike France and the United States, which have shortages. Furthermore, the demand for the pound is currently strong, resulting in a strong pound, while the dollar and franc pale in comparison and repeatedly weaken. (4th, Reuters)

(London) The British government's recent debt repayment method is widely regarded as another clear proof of the stability of the British financial position. The Financial News stated that the amount of debt currently borrowed by the British government is exactly the same as the original exchange equalization amount, which shows the British government's intention to place the equalization fund on a permanent basis. It is expected that the interest rate on treasury bills will be reduced. (4th, Reuters)

(London) The British government announced today that it will raise £150 million in 3% interest bonds, to be repaid between 25 and 35 years, issued at a price of 98. The proceeds of the bonds are intended to repay the £10.05 million in 4% interest treasury bills due on April 15th. This move will save the Ministry of Finance £1 million per year. The remaining £45 million from the new bonds will be used to repay short-term debt. (4th, Reuters)

(London) The unemployment situation in the UK continues to ease. According to statistics released today, since March 19th, more than 10 million people have found jobs, aged from 16 to 64. This number is 117,000 more than the previous month and 644,000 more than last year. However, there are still 2.2 million unemployed people nationwide. (3rd, Reuters)

(Washington) A recent report from the US Treasury Department shows a shortage of 250 million yuan in the first nine months of the current fiscal year, which is causing great anxiety to the authorities. Expenditures during this period totaled approximately 5 billion yuan, while income was 2.305 billion yuan. Public debt at the end of March this year was 26,157,509,000 yuan, compared to 21,362,464,000 yuan last year. Treasury Secretary Morgenthau stated today that he is currently studying government revenue from alcohol taxes. Alcohol tax revenue is currently lower than expected. The Treasury Department is considering whether reducing the tax rate on alcohol can increase revenue, but will submit its recommendations to Congress later. The budget shortage may hinder various government plans, and there may be an important announcement about trial measures tomorrow. Market participants expect the US Treasury Department to issue long-term bonds to exchange for the 4th Liberty Bonds due on April 15th. (3rd, Reuters)

The New Situation in European Politics (Correspondence from France) 86

The Soviet Union Influences All of Europe, Austria-Hungary Struggles Vigorously

The Conflict Between France and Germany is Intense, and Ill Feelings Between France and Italy are Rising

Since the establishment of the Franco-Soviet Commercial Treaty, the general diplomatic situation in Europe has taken a sharp turn. The diplomatic fronts of the past show a tendency to be reorganized. Originally, the European problem, for many years, has still been centered on France and Germany. Every rise and fall, every victory and defeat, has been based on these two countries. This remains the case after the World War. In France's view, it is best to be able to restrain Germany, and the longer the restraint, the better. The weapons she uses—the weapons to restrain Germany—are two: one is the Treaty of Versailles, and the other is the League of Nations. The Treaty of Versailles is an agreement that restricts Germany's upward development. This agreement is not only recognized by the Allied countries, but Germany itself has also signed it. The League of Nations originally included all the capitalist countries in the world (except the United States). Germany also joined it, but he withdrew at the end of last year. In fact, the Treaty of Versailles, especially the provisions for reparations, prompted Germany to borrow heavily from the United States and promoted Germany's recovery, leading to France's strong enemy today. The smaller European countries were originally intended by France to be satellites to jointly deal with Germany. Unexpectedly, on January 26th of this year, the German-Polish Non-Aggression Pact was concluded, and France's containment strategy in the east has been greatly reduced. Recently, Austria-Hungary has also become particularly close to Italy. While there may not be any great political magic, it is indeed a very new movement in the economy. In addition to strictly preventing Germany, France must also prepare to deal with Italy.

Of course, France wants to firmly hold onto Britain. However, Britain's traditional foreign policy is to support the two major powers in Europe and is unwilling to over-assist France and suppress Germany. Therefore, France has to change its old strategy, no longer deepening its ill feelings towards the Soviet Union, and taking the opportunity to approach the Soviet Union. The general reason given on the surface for France's anti-Soviet stance is due to ideological relations and the Soviet Union's advocacy of world revolution. In fact, the Soviet Union's previous assessment of the place where the revolution would break out in Europe was not in France. So why did France feel so opposed to the Soviet Union? Because since the [Brest-Litovsk] German-Russian Treaty was concluded, Germany and the Soviet Union have been very close. At the same time, Germany often used diplomacy with the Soviet Union to maneuver between the Allied countries when the Social Democratic Party was in power. The trade relations between Germany and the Soviet Union were also very close. According to military intelligence, Germany even manufactured some important weapons in Russia. While this may not be true, it is enough to provoke France's psychology of suppressing Germany and thus hating Russia. Thus, a state of opposition always existed between France and Russia. Furthermore, after the October Revolution in Russia, it completely denied and refused to repay the 6.44 billion gold francs of debt owed to France before the war. Also, French private investments in the Baku oil fields and other important industries were all confiscated. The Soviet Union believed that this was a matter of course and the fairest move. France, on the other hand, believed that it was an infringement of the sacred and inviolable right of ownership. The two sides have been confronting each other for more than a decade, and it is still unresolved.

Recently, France and the Soviet Union have swept away their former barriers and turned to a tendency of friendship, without mentioning the resolution of past economic outstanding issues as a condition. According to the current situation in France, even if those debts are not repaid at all, it will not cause much damage to France. However, if its most feared enemy rises up, France's losses will naturally be greater. Moreover, Italy has implicitly formed its own system, which is also against the Versailles system, and is almost in a state of semi-withdrawal from the League of Nations. Therefore, France cannot but find other countries in Europe. It so happened that the Soviet Union relaxed its attempt at world revolution, and its relations with Germany deteriorated again. This is why it tried its best to win over the Soviet Union. Needless to say, this is to weaken Germany's influence, and vice versa, to increase France's diplomatic assistance. There is also the claim that the League of Nations will invite the Soviet Union to join, and the Soviet Union has not refused. If this really comes true, international disputes will present a new situation. (March 2, 1934, in Paris)

○　　○　　○　　○

Japanese Activities in Europe World Electric News Agency 87

Economic and Political Advancement, All Countries Feel Its Threat

Using Money for Malicious Propaganda Unfavorable to Our Country

Paris Correspondence, September 18th is not only a date in Chinese history, but also a date in world history. Since that time, China has temporarily lost the four northeastern provinces, and even the area sixty miles outside Beiping has become enemy territory. A portion of Shanghai's prosperity has been reduced to ashes. Good medicine tastes bitter, and for China, it must be said to be a great lesson for revival. However, the significance of September 18th is not limited to the Far East. One point that must be noted first is that, on the whole, Europeans are still somewhat isolated from the situation in the Far East. When the news of the bombing of the Beida Camp reached Europe, the general European public, as the President of the University of Paris told reporters, felt as if they had been struck by a bolt from the blue. Later, a series of bad news further deepened the astonishment of the people of various countries. However, the four northeastern provinces are too far away from here. Not to mention other countries, even the United States and Russia, which have the closest relationship with China, are still trapped in their own situations and unable to act. Therefore, although there were resolutions in Geneva and warnings from a few strong powers, in fact, they just said what they said and did what they did. Those who sympathize sympathize, and those who suffer continue to suffer. The world economic crisis paralyzed the great powers. China relied on others without any resistance. Both of these things were seen clearly by the Japanese. Thus, the four northeastern provinces became the situation they are today. This situation, apart from a few news reporters, diplomats, travelers, businessmen, and politicians with a truly far-sighted vision, is not clearly understood by the general European public based solely on newspaper reports. In other words, in the minds of the general European public, if the significance of September 18th is limited to China's loss of four provinces, then the significance of September 18th is not deep enough. Because most of them are really isolated from the Sino-Japanese incident. Moreover, over the years (especially after September 18th), Japan's foreign propaganda has tarnished China to the point of not being a country, so that many Europeans, even if they do not believe it, can at least silently acquiesce to Japan's behavior.

However, after September 18th, there were many other things that Europeans could not but pay attention to. Because these things happened after September 18th, because they happened in Europe closer to home, and because they happened in Europe itself, Europeans gradually felt their immediate interests. Even gradually felt what the September 18th tragedy had at the time, but was ignored because they were too far away, is [Japan's Ambition]. The best evidence of such feelings among Europeans is Mussolini's article [Eastern Dark Clouds], published in January this year.

The activities of the Japanese, who expressed this ambition, in Europe can be viewed from two aspects: economic and political. Let's first talk about the economic aspect. Anyone who has been in Europe for a long time can see the abundance of Japanese goods on the market in the past two or three years. Not to mention many Japanese goods that impersonate Chinese art and Chinese porcelain. This kind of Japanese goods has been around for a long time, although more and more people are seeing through them. However, because the price is really too cheap, it is different from the price of genuine Chinese art and Chinese porcelain displayed in antique shops in Paris and London. Therefore, there are always people who buy them. In addition, there are some items, such as camphor, that Europe does not produce. Because China is unable to compete with Japan, and even has to buy Japanese goods itself, Japan has always monopolized these items on the European market, and it is not just starting today. However, the Japanese goods that have increased in the European market in the past two or three years are not like this. If you are not careful in a shoe store in Paris, you will buy rubber-soled Japanese-made sports shoes. Many Japanese watches can also be found in watch stores, and beautifully decorated and surprisingly cheap Japanese biscuits can be found in food stores. These food products are not lacking in Britain and France, but because the products made in Britain and France are too good, the prices are too expensive. Since the world economic panic, the purchasing power of the general British and French people is really not enough. On the contrary, the original price of Japanese goods is already low, and coupled with the sudden drop in the external value of the Japanese yen, a large number of goods are dumped into Europe. Even with tariffs, the selling price can still be much cheaper than the prices of domestic goods in various countries. This is why this result occurs. The above are just a few examples to prove that Japanese goods are gradually invading the major markets in Europe. The situation in Paris and London is like this, not to mention other Central European countries.

Japan's economic development in various parts of Europe, just from the few obvious examples mentioned above, is already worth paying attention to. However, there is something more surprising to Europeans, which is the Japanese activity near the Middle Eastern route, which Europeans regard as colonies or spheres of influence.

A few months ago, the Ta Kung Pao published an article listing the economic conflicts between Japan and Britain in Australia. The increasingly dangerous economic competition between Japan and Britain in India is also a fact known to the world. In Britain's attitude towards Japan, these facts have their serious significance, echoing the completion of the British naval base in Singapore. However, there are some other facts that the world does not know much about, and because of the geographical distance closer to Europe, and because of the historical relationship Europeans have a special psychology towards this, they make European politicians, industrialists, businessmen, and even the general public feel flustered, and especially arouse their fears of the [Yellow Peril]. These facts occur on the coast of the Red Sea, especially in Ethiopia.

This kingdom, located in eastern Africa and south of Egypt, has an area of 1.2 million square kilometers and a population of more than 11 million. The European powers, because its industries are not yet developed and its land is still waiting to be developed, have always regarded it as a competition arena for political and economic interests. Two and a half years ago, when Ethiopian King Haile Selassie I was crowned, all countries sent envoys to congratulate him, including Japan. Afterwards, the Ethiopian King sent a delegation to Japan to return the courtesy. Then, the then head envoy, the current Ethiopian Minister of Foreign Affairs, started the first step of industrial and commercial cooperation negotiations between the two countries with the Japanese government. The purpose was to encourage Japanese industrialists and businessmen to develop land in various places in Ethiopia and promote the new development of agriculture and industry in a certain area of the country. Was this negotiation desired by Japan, or requested by Ethiopia? We can ignore it. In short, as a result of the negotiations, the former Ethiopian Minister of Foreign Affairs signed a new tariff agreement in Tokyo with the Japanese government last year, which was favorable to Japanese commerce. At the same time, it was decided to immediately send a technical team composed of agricultural experts, businessmen, and export trade experts to Ethiopia for on-the-spot investigation. Soon, the Ethiopian government issued a declaration, willing to exempt taxes and give about 60 hectares of good land to Japanese immigrants, as a full test for them to plant cotton. In addition, there are other special privileges granted for new industrial establishment tests of the same nature. When these tests are successful, further cooperation with Japanese technology will be needed. Last year, this test period has come to an end. The operation of the Japanese is becoming more and more convenient. In order to encourage land development, to resist the import of European manufactured products and to promote the cultivation of cotton and other plants, the Ethiopian government decided to continue to accommodate the requests of Japanese businessmen on a large scale and allow their immigration. In addition, the Ethiopian King intends to choose a Japanese woman as the Queen, and the Japanese side has candidates such as Viscount Kuroda's daughter. Therefore, up to now, Japan's economic activities in Ethiopia cannot but be said to be a great success.

But before the Japanese forces invaded, the market of Ethiopia was originally in the hands of the Americans. Later, the British used Indian cotton yarn to gradually replace the Americans. Therefore, Ethiopia has become a market for the sales of British colonial products. Recently, the import value of this British colonial cotton yarn still accounts for about 50% of the Ethiopian customs statistics. In the future, after Japanese-operated yarn mills and so on are established in Ethiopia, these British colonial products and the goods of other European powers will be completely cut off from sales in Ethiopia. (To be continued)

One Scene of Hui Bandits Attempting to Occupy Tacheng Special Telegram from Tacheng 88

| After Yao Huating Led Reinforcements to Repel |

Ma Heying, the remnant of the Hui bandit Ma Zhongying from Xinjiang, wanted to attack Tacheng from Altay with great force. Governor Sheng, seeing that no one was in command of the garrison in Tacheng, appointed General Yao Huating as the Brigadier General Commander of Tacheng's city defense in order to plan the blocking attack. Unfortunately, the announcement

Portrait of Yao Huating, Who Made Great Efforts to Protect Tacheng 89

was too late. On the 5th of last month, the bandits had already occupied Emin County and cut off the route for reinforcements from the provincial capital. At that time, Yao was on his way. Upon hearing that Emin had fallen, he bypassed the mountain road alone and advanced at great risk. He arrived in Tacheng at 2:00 AM on the 7th. At that time, Tacheng was not in communication with the provincial capital. He immediately summoned the military and civilians to work together to defend the city and await reinforcements. The morale was boosted. On the morning of the 8th, more than 3,000 bandits attacked Tacheng. They attacked the city day and night for more than ten times. The garrison barely held on, but all attempts failed. On the night of the 10th, the bandits set fire to the surroundings of each city gate and climbed the city walls with ladders. The momentum was great. Yao personally supervised the military and civilians, fought several times, and killed more than 300 bandits under the city. On the 11th, our reinforcements arrived by car. On the 12th, Yao led all the troops to attack together. After a day of street fighting, the bandits finally could not hold on and retreated to Emin. On the 14th, Yao's army attacked Emin again, and the bandits fled southeast. This fierce battle with the bandits was unprecedented in Xinjiang. The aftermath is now being handled. The tens of thousands of people in Tacheng are greatly indebted to General Yao's efforts to protect them and have telegraphed the chairman and governor of the provincial capital to retain him permanently in Tacheng. (Tacheng Chamber of Commerce, Xinjiang, January 1, 1934)

Setting Up a Machine-Made Porcelain Factory in Jiangxi Province 94

A Full Capital of One Million

Shao De's Proposed Plan Content

Nanchang Correspondence: The large-scale porcelain company of Jiangxi Province, since Xiong Shi and Finance Minister Kong Xiangxi agreed to establish it, all parties have been actively proceeding. The Department of Finance has now located a large open space near St. John's School in Xunyang to be used as the factory site. The capital amount is one million yuan, half of which will be allocated by the Ministry of Industry, and the remaining five hundred thousand yuan is said to be raised from commercial shares. The internal organization of the company is divided into three major departments: teaching, testing, and manufacturing. In order to facilitate work and save expenses, it is decided to merge the Provincial Pottery School and the Pottery Testing Institute into the teaching department. According to this organizational plan, the original name is [Machine-Made Pottery Factory]. The plan was proposed by Shao Dehui, the current director of the Jiangxi Pottery Testing Institute, and the content is as follows: Jiangxi Jingdezhen is a porcelain-producing area, and manufacturing relies entirely on manual labor, resulting in excessive costs, unable to compete with the low cost of foreign porcelain manufactured by machines. Therefore, foreign porcelain has been invading the market for a long time, and it is feared that it will be completely occupied. Only by establishing a large-scale factory and using machine manufacturing can we compete with it. Moreover, Jingdezhen is the largest porcelain-producing area in China. The transportation there is not convenient, and the bad habits of the workers are also very deep. To develop, it is necessary to move the location. The counties of Xingzi and Yujiang in Jiangxi produce the most porcelain clay, all downstream of Jingdezhen. If the porcelain factory is established in Jiujiang, the transportation of raw materials and the sales of products will be very suitable. Therefore, it is hoped that a machine-made pottery factory will be established near the river in Jiujiang. According to the medium-scale plan, a capital of approximately four million silver dollars is required, of which 550,000 will be for real estate and machinery fixed capital, and 150,000 will be for circulating business capital. All equipment methods and profit budgets are listed below: (A) Factory Equipment (1) Clay Factory Building, one-story, construction materials cost 10,700 foreign yuan. Two sets each of stone wheel wet grinding machine, large drum-shaped pulverizer, and small drum-shaped pulverizer. One set of continuous drum-shaped pulverizer. Han Paintings Discovered in Zichuan County, Shandong Province 95

Preserved in the People's Education Hall in Yuncheng

Jinan Correspondence: In recent years, Han Dynasty paintings and ancient steles have been frequently discovered in the area north of Zichuan County, but most are incomplete. This spring, Li Guojie, a villager from Jia Ping Township north of the city, unearthed many bricks and stones while digging soil at the edge of the field. The township head, Che Chunyuan, believed that the bricks were all hemp bricks and the stone carvings had excellent patterns, presuming it was an ancient tomb. He immediately reported it to the People's Education Hall. On the 30th of last month, the director of the hall, Liu Kedian, together with Lu Hongzao and Meng Junsheng, members of the Antiquities Preservation Committee, personally went to investigate. They saw a total of six stones, on which were carved chariots, horses, people, and beasts, with vermilion color still discernible. They were also inscribed with the nine characters [These people and horses all eat from the Heavenly Spring Granary], confirming it to be a complete Han Dynasty tomb door. The hall has now negotiated with the Li family and will transport it to the city soon for preservation, so that those who study ancient history and culture can refer to it. (2nd)

Suzhou 96

Robbery and Assault in Guangfu Township 97

In Zhengjiawan, the eighth picture of the twenty-eighth capital of Guangfu Township, at the home of villager Zheng A'er, seven or eight bandits arrived on the afternoon of the third, tied up Zheng A'er, and burned his wife, Zhu, in the breast area with fire, and beat his sister-in-law, Chen, in the waist. As a result, more than two hundred yuan of silver and clothing were robbed, and the bandits fled towards the edge of Taihu Lake.

Zhang Yipeng and others request tax reduction 98

Local gentry Zhang Yipeng and others believe that the tax burden in Wuxian County is heavier than in other counties. When the field price was more than one hundred yuan per mu, it already exceeded one percent. Now that the rural areas are bankrupt and the field price has plummeted, each mu is only worth more than thirty foreign yuan, but the land price tax paid is still about one yuan and six jiao per mu, which the people cannot bear. They specially submitted a request to the provincial government's civil and financial departments yesterday (4th) to reduce it when compiling the budget for the 23rd year, so as to alleviate the people's burden.

Wuxi 99

Liu Zhuomin's case opens for trial; Gu Weilai comes to Wuxi for questioning 100

Since the Liu Zhuomin case occurred, involving Li Shuyun, the wife of former Jiangsu Provincial Civil Affairs Director Gu Renfa, and her daughter, they were jointly interrogated and detained by the local court, which further triggered the issue of Gu Renfa's bigamy and marriage fraud. This has been repeatedly reported in this newspaper. Yesterday (4th) afternoon at 2 o'clock, the case was scheduled for court. The procuratorate had previously ordered Gu Renfa to be summoned to court for questioning. However, Gu had not arrived in Wuxi to report to the court by 5 o'clock. The Capital Supervisory Yuan believed that the case was serious and that although Gu Renfa had resigned to take responsibility, it was still necessary to impeach him according to law so as to give him appropriate punishment. Therefore, they specially sent two supervisory committee members (local people), Yang Tianji and Duan Honggang, to Wuxi to investigate yesterday morning. After arriving in Wuxi, the two stayed at Room 21 of the Washington Hotel. The county magistrate of this county, Yan Shenyu, went to the hotel to pay his respects upon hearing the news. Committee members Yang and others inquired in detail about the course of the case, and Magistrate Yan reported it one by one. Later, Magistrate Yan hosted a luncheon at the hotel. At 2:40 in the afternoon, Yan accompanied Yang and others to the county court to meet with Chief Procurator Qian Chengjun to inquire about everything and review the case files. Afterwards, they went to Huishan and other places to visit scenic spots. At 3:30, the Supervisory Yuan sent another investigation specialist, Ma Zhen [Zi Tailong], to Wuxi, who stayed at the Wuxi Hotel. After a short rest, he went directly to the county court and left after about half an hour. At about 5 o'clock in the afternoon, Chief Qian opened the court for interrogation. In addition to Gu Renfa's failure to appear in court, those who were summoned and appeared in court included Zhang Yun, the police chief of the Public Security Bureau, and police officers Chen Hongjin, Liang Zhengshan, Chen Jimin, Ji Huashan, and Ge Deming. According to their testimony, when they searched Liu Zhuomin's residence at the Donghu Hotel on that day, they found two letters in his luggage, one addressed to a friend in Jiangxi and the other from Rong Zhen to her husband, Liu Zhuomin, as well as a blank sheet of paper with Gu Renfa's private seal on it, etc. As a result, the court ordered them all to be dismissed. After Li Shuyun was imprisoned, she hired two lawyers, Zhang Shizhao and Chao Kun, to draft a complaint accusing Gu of bigamy and marriage fraud. Yesterday, Lawyer Chao came to Wuxi from Shanghai and met with Li Shuyun at the detention center. Li immediately urged Lawyer Chao to submit the complaint as soon as possible to redress her grievances. Lawyer Chao replied that this matter would be discussed with Lawyer Zhang before proceeding.

Grand Occasion of Children's Memorial Day 101

All sectors of this county are preparing to celebrate the Children's Day Memorial, and County Education Bureau Hua Jinji was appointed as the preparation director, preparing everything. Yesterday (4th) morning at 9 o'clock, a celebration meeting was held at the Zhongnan Grand Theater in the city, with more than two thousand children and hundreds of representatives from all walks of life attending. The entire ceremony was performed as scheduled. After the chairman of the county party department, Committee Member Gui, County Magistrate Yan of the county government, and Director Zang of the county education bureau delivered speeches, Pan Ren gave a speech, followed by speeches from Xu Xi, a student from the attached primary school (male), Lin Tong, a student from County One (male), Ji Mian, a student from Sanhuang Street Primary School (female), Gu Jiheng, a student from the attached primary school (female), and Qian Jiaxiu, a student from Jingzhi Girls' Middle School (female). The language was extremely concise and their spoken Mandarin was very fluent, winning applause from all the students. After the speeches, sweets were presented, and Committee Member Gui, County Magistrate Yan, and Director Zang distributed sweets and toys to the male and female students who spoke. Then, a film was shown to add to the fun, and the meeting adjourned at 11 o'clock. On this day, entertainment venues such as the Zhongnan, Wuxi Yaoji, Xinguang, Qingsheng, and First Taichung East theaters all had discounted daytime shows to welcome children to watch plays. All stores selling children's items also offered discounts. The county library and others held children's happiness exhibitions, and the public sports ground at Xule Park and the People's Education Hall were open all day. Various schools also held funfairs and achievement exhibitions. In the afternoon, the rain reduced children's activities.

Changzhou 102

Opening of coffin for autopsy in the case of murdering husband 103

Jiang Jiangshi, a woman from Xihonglin in the 14th district of Wujin County, was naturally lewd and had an affair. Recently, she took advantage of her husband Jiang Xikun being bedridden and gave him poison to swallow, causing his death. She hastily prepared him for burial. Zhenjiang 107

Hu Jianchun Commits Suicide by Poison 108

Hu Jianchun, a prominent figure in Zhenjiang's business community, was upright and enthusiastic about public welfare. He dedicated almost all of his energy to social undertakings such as the water company, fire brigade, school, chamber of commerce, commercial group, and charity hall. Recently, due to overwork and mental weakness, and because the water company he ran lacked funds for development, he became weary of the world. He took poison at one o'clock in the morning on the 2nd. By the time his family discovered it, he was unconscious and beyond rescue. He died at eight o'clock in the morning on the 3rd at the age of 52. He had no personal debts. He listed all the various undertakings he ran in his will and entrusted friends to continue to maintain them. It is now scheduled to be placed in a coffin on the evening of the 4th. All groups believe that Mr. Hu contributed to society and is worthy of admiration by the world, and they plan to prepare a grand memorial service and erect a monument to commemorate him.

Yangzhou 109

Petition of Salt Merchants on Both Banks of Huainan 110

Salt merchants on the banks of Xiang, Hubei, West Anhui, and West Anhui appointed representatives last year to petition for the revocation of the order after the Ministry of Finance abolished the method of exempting tax supplements for submerged consumption. They spent months running around Beijing and Shanghai, but did not receive a response. This year, a new scale was adopted, and the government failed to clearly deduct the tare weight. Merchants used this as an excuse to attack and deduct the merchants' capital. The Ministry of Finance also imposed additional salt bank taxes, causing problems at all levels that could not be resolved. Recently, the Hunan Inspection Office forcibly ordered Hunan merchants to set up a Changsha salt sales office according to the Hubei bank method, prepay ten tax periods each month, and sell at reduced prices. The salt merchants believe that this is related to the survival of the business and that they are in danger of bankruptcy. Because the Salt Affairs Office and the Inspection Office convened various bank officials and staff in Nanjing for a meeting, the representatives went to Nanjing to petition. This shows the decline of commerce. It is unknown whether the authorities can understand the merchants' situation.

Yangzhou-Zhong Long-Distance Bus Begins Service 111

The Yangzhou-Zhong long-distance bus has changed its route, rerouting through Xixiang via Dayi in Jiangdu, entering Tianchang and Tongcheng in Anhui, and then heading directly to Jiangzheng Town and reaching Qingjiang, taking years. It began service on the 3rd. Yangzhou and Qingjiang operate once a day, and the one-way fare to Yangzhou and Qingjiang is 7 yuan and 2 jiao, with round-trip tickets sold at a 30% discount.

Provincial Order to Investigate and Arrest Smugglers of Opium by Ship 112

The Jiangdu County Government received a secret order from the provincial government stating that according to confidential reports, Deng Beichao had sent a letter to Hankou, informing him to move to 26 Rulaizhu, Yangzhou, instructing him to wait for the arrival of Jianghua and Jiangan Jiang ships five times to Hankou and transport twelve pieces of opium per ship. The county was ordered to investigate, arrest, and interrogate. Specifically, on the morning of the 3rd, the county secretly dispatched the police team leader Zhu Hui and the political police chief Wang Dongchen to arrest and escort him to the county at the address. Director Tan interrogated him in court. Deng confessed that he was 20 years old, from Huangpi, Hubei. He used to be at the Chuanjiang Long Opium Company on Xin Shen Road in Hankou, collecting debts from sailors on various Yangtze River ships. He had come to Yangzhou and Zhenjiang to collect debts from sailors who owed money and could not go to Hankou to avoid them. He had just arrived in Yangzhou around the first month of the lunar year, intending to explore the debts. He also confessed the surnames Yao and Chen and planned to seek employment in Yangzhou. The interrogator asked whether he had relatives and friends, but Deng refused to confess and denied sending a letter to Hankou, saying that the handwriting could be compared. He was ordered to be handed over to the county detective team for detention pending verification.

Jiashan

Shen Liaoru and His Wife Tragically Drowned 113

Shen Ziru, a native of this county, has been working in Fujian political circles. During the 19th Route Army mutiny last year, Shen Ziru resolutely broke away from the rebel party, which was deeply trusted by his superiors. During the Qingming Festival this year, he took his family back to his hometown to visit his relatives. On the day before yesterday, he went to the countryside to sweep the tombs. When the boat passed Xiamu Lake, it was raining heavily and the northwest wind was strong, and the waves were raging. The boatman accidentally caused the boat to capsize. Shen Ziru and his wife both drowned because they did not know how to swim. The three boatmen were fortunately familiar with the water and survived. This is also very tragic.

Rice Boat Robbed En Route 114

Zhou Genfa and other boatmen from Changshu, who operated six rice boats from Shanghai to this county, were fully loaded with goods when they sailed to the vicinity of Suzhen at midnight on the 31st. Suddenly, two bandit boats came head-on, threatening to stop sailing with guns. More than a dozen bandits jumped out, looted the rice boats one by one, and all money and white rice were robbed. The boat crew was unable to resist and shouted for help. At that time, Wang, the village chief of Tagang Village, heard the sound and rang the gong. The farmers in the village woke up in shock and rushed to the scene of the incident, surrounding the bandit boat and fighting with the boat crew. The bandits gradually became unable to support themselves. The village chief encouraged his remaining courage and captured two bandits alive. Seeing that the bandit leader had been captured, the remaining bandits fled in droves. Not long after, one bandit was also chased and captured. The village chief immediately detained the three bandits and a bandit boat and handed them over to the local public security bureau, who transferred them to this county court for interrogation. They confessed that there were sixteen accomplices, staying in various districts of this county, suddenly looting. The authorities of this county specially ordered a unified and strict arrest yesterday.

Huzhou

Detailed Account of the Weaving Workers' Strike 115

The labor-capital dispute between weaving workers and management due to wage discounts has lasted for two months. Although the Party and government have repeatedly mediated, the workers have been difficult to resolve when they do not obey. On the afternoon of the 2nd of this month, the factory workers' forced shutdown of zero-machine workers resulted in a tragic incident. The circumstances are as follows: Huzhou weaving workers have always been divided into two types: factory workers and zero-machine workers. Since the wage discount labor-capital dispute, the factory workers have not resumed work. The zero-machine workers believe that although they are both weaving workers, they are forced to make a living. After the provincial party committee came to Huzhou to investigate, they followed the county government's instructions and resumed work first. The factory workers were very angry when they heard about it and went to stop them. The two sides had a conflict, injuring five zero-machine workers, and one person was arrested by the rebels. Therefore, each zero-machine household was in danger and went to the county government to request protection. After hearing the news, the county government immediately dispatched a task force to suppress the situation and rescue the arrested machine households. The large group of factory workers heard that the machine households had arrived at the county government, so they tracked them down. At that time, the county government gate had a task force guarding it. When the factory workers arrived, they were blocked by the team. At that time, there were too many people and the order was disrupted. There were rioters who intended to rush into the iron gate. The guards tried their best to stop them, but it was difficult to support them. There were even those who tried to grab guns. Seeing this dangerous situation, the task force fired into the air as a warning. Unexpectedly, the stray bullets from the gunfire killed two workers and injured one. Seeing that they had caused trouble, the factory workers were still unwilling to leave and were still demonstrating in the vicinity of the county government. At that time, each store saw that the order of the street was disrupted and heard gunshots, fearing that it would be affected, so they closed their doors one after another. By five o'clock in the afternoon, each street in the city was unusually calm. After the incident, County Magistrate Dai immediately reported to the provincial government by long-distance telephone. He also temporarily imposed martial law, ordering the military police to patrol closely, adding sentries near the county government, and posting notices to persuade the machine workers.

Ningbo 116

Elder Brother Poisonously Kills Younger Brother 117

Guo Juren Lin Kefeng's third son, Mingshan, of the seventh district of Zhenhai, is over thirty years old. Because he does not engage in proper business, he is economically distressed. He often demanded from his father, resulting in discord between father and sons and brothers. The other day, Mingshan again asked his father for money. While they were arguing, his elder brother Xingmo happened to enter from outside, saw it, and scolded loudly. Therefore, there was an argument with Mingshan, followed by violence. After being persuaded by neighbors, they dispersed separately. However, Mingshan was unconvinced. Not long after, he returned, holding a pack of matches, full of anger, seeming to want to commit arson. At this time, his second brother Xinglian returned home and twisted Mingshan. For a time, the brothers twisted into a ball, fighting violently. Fortunately, relatives gave Mingshan two yuan to calm the matter. However, Mingshan hated his second brother even more. That night, Mingshan carried a sharp blade, but could not find Xingmo and Xinglian, unable to vent his hatred. The next day, he sought an excuse to intimidate his father with a knife. Fortunately, his father avoided him, unharmed. Kefeng could no longer bear it, so he consulted with relatives to discuss ways to expel him. Xingmo also gathered his cousins Yao Arong, blacksmith Hu Yangchun, and Wang Yichen, each hiding weapons. That evening, they rushed into Mingshan's room. At this time, Mingshan was already asleep. Hu Yangchun immediately hit Mingshan's head hard with an iron plate. Mingshan woke up in extreme pain and shouted for help. The family members were alarmed and rushed to see the situation, horrified, and hurriedly scolded and stopped them. However, the crowd was murderous and did not listen. They dragged Mingshan to the ground, first cutting off his two feet, then stuffing cotton into Mingshan's throat, and then using a hemp bag to store the corpse and dragged it to Xinqi tou and threw it on the beach. After the crowd of murderers returned home, they intimidated Ke Ling, forcing him to admit to killing his son. Ke Ming had no choice but to admit it with tears. As for Mingshan's corpse, because the east wind suddenly rose the day before yesterday, it had drifted away with the tide.

Haimen 118

Shipping Industry Petitions to Abolish Boat License Donations 119

The Education Bureau previously received approval from the Ministry of Finance and Education in the spring of the 20th year to collect boat license donations to support educational expenses. The county committee Chen Zhao (ie Chen Sicao) was responsible for it. Since Chen took over, malpractices have been rampant, such as forging boat licenses and overcharging donations, totaling as much as 4,000 yuan. For a time, complaints were heard everywhere. The boat owners repeatedly filed complaints to the province and county. In January of this year, the county investigated and dismissed him, and Yang Douding was approved to take over. However, the boat owners believed that Yang was Chen Zhao's personal friend, and it would be difficult to avoid repeating the same mistakes in the future. They still unanimously expressed their opposition and petitioned the county government yesterday (2nd) to forward it to the provincial government to permanently abolish this boat license donation, so as to alleviate the people's suffering.

Local News

Over Ten Thousand Children Celebrated Children's Day Enthusiastically at the Municipal Government Yesterday 120

The Mayor Hosted All the City's Children

Cai Yuanpei and Li Shizeng Spoke at the Venue

Women's Groups and Lake Society Held Celebrations

Cai Yuanpei's Wife and Others Gave Speeches

Yesterday was the fourth official Children's Day in our country. Over ten thousand children from all walks of life in the city participated in the celebration ceremony of the municipal government, and the mayor hosted the children and met with the children's representatives. Cai Yuanpei and Li Shizeng specially attended the meeting and delivered speeches. Although it was drizzling yesterday, the children's spirits were unusually uplifted. At 2:00 p.m., the Women's National Goods Year Movement Committee held a memorial meeting at Lake Society. The enthusiasm for this year's Children's Day celebration was greater than in previous years. Details of each situation are recorded as follows:

Various Circles Hold Celebration Ceremonies 121

(A Glimpse of the Venue) The celebration ceremony for Children's Day, organized by various circles, was held in front of the Municipal Government Building. A bright red banner with golden characters read [Shanghai Municipal Celebration of Children's Day and Mayor's Reception for Children] was hung across the entrance of the Municipal Government. The plaza was divided into four sections: General, Charity, Factory, and School. When children arrived at East Municipal Government Road, they were led in by receptionists from their respective groups. The area was surrounded by wooden fences. The Third Squadron of the Municipal Public Security Bureau's Police Brigade and patrol officers from the Second Precinct of the Seventh District were dispatched to maintain order. Two ambulances from the Municipal Health Bureau and the entire rescue team were stationed on-site. There was also a performance stage and a fire brigade observation tower in front of the plaza. The rostrum was set up on the stone steps in front of the Municipal Government, equipped with a public address system that clearly broadcast speeches, audible throughout the venue. Chinese and foreign film companies were present to film the event, creating a lively atmosphere.

Participating Children

In addition to representatives from various organizations, yesterday's participants included students from over a hundred schools, such as He'an, Guangming, Zhengxiu, Minzhi, Private Shangxiao, Danhua, Fan'ai, Jie'ru, Shanghai University Affiliated Elementary School, Sanyu, Boren, Hudong, Huaxia, Banjiang, Pusong, Ningbo, and Second Elementary School. Factory children included labor children representatives from the Sixth District Water and Electricity Workers' Union, Fifth District Cigarette Workers' Union, Tenth District Cotton Textile Workers' Union, Fourth District Electrical Appliance Workers' Union, Western-style Clothing Industry Union, Cotton Weaving Industry Union, and Western-style Gold and Silverware Industry Union. Charity children included those from the Longhua Orphanage, the Chinese Relief for Women and Children Student Corps, the Zhabei Civilian Education and Confinement Institute, the Zhabei Charity Group, the Hui'er Orphanage, as well as ordinary children from various circles, totaling no less than ten thousand people.

Convention Staff

The presidium included Cai Hongtian from the Municipal Party Headquarters, Mayor Wu Tiecheng, Wu Xingya, Director of the Social Affairs Bureau, Wen Hong'en, Director of the Public Security Bureau, Pan Gongzhan, Director of the Education Bureau (represented by Hu), Li Ting'an, Director of the Health Bureau (represented by Shen Gao), Hu Shuyi from the Children's Welfare Association, Wang Guanyi from the China Child Welfare Association, Lin Kecong, He Xiya, and Sun Daosheng from the Women's National Goods Year Movement Committee. The master of ceremonies was Yu Pu, the general commander was Zhang Tingrong, the school children commander was Yang Zhi, the factory children commander was [blank], the charity group children commander was Yang Maorong, the ordinary children commander was Wang Guanyi, the chief receptionist was Qiu Xisheng, the model children receptionist was Zhou Wanghe, the foreign guests receptionist was Jiang Heqi, the gift administrator was Qian Fugong, and there were over fifty receptionists.

Mayor's Speech

The celebration ceremony opened at 9:30 AM. After performing the rituals, Mayor Wu, the chairman, delivered an encouraging speech, stating, "Today is Children's Day, so we are holding this Children's Day celebration assembly here today. The significance of Children's Day is to awaken the people of the nation, especially parents with children, to pay attention to loving and nurturing children. Children should be made aware of their relationship with the country and the nation. It must be understood that children belong to the country and society. The children of today are the future masters of China. They are the new hope for the life of the Chinese nation. Therefore, the survival of China and the safety of the nation's future depend entirely on the children of today. China has been weak to this day, and we are facing unprecedented national difficulties. If we want to save ourselves from this unprecedented national crisis, we must make the country rich and strong. If we want to make the country rich and strong, we must first revive the Chinese nation. In other words, reviving the Chinese nation is for the purpose of making China rich and strong. Only when China is rich and strong can we save ourselves from today's national crisis. Our China has a long and glorious history of more than four thousand years and is the earliest civilized nation in the world. If we can pay attention to the protection and education of children, and give them practical training in their thoughts, habits, bodies, and morals, thoroughly transform their lives, and fully develop their strengths, so that each and every child of today will become a healthy, powerful, and useful good citizen, and each generation will be stronger than the last, then I believe that not only can the national crisis be resolved, but our Chinese nation will also definitely be able to revive, and our China will definitely be able to become rich and strong. So, let us all wish the Republic of China a long life, the Chinese nation a long life, and the Chinese Nationalist Party a long life!"

Cai Yuanpei's Speech

Cai Yuanpei's speech briefly stated, "Today is April 4th, which is Chinese Children's Day. Our National Day is October 10th, which is called Double Ten Day, so Children's Day can also be called Double Four Day. The first four characters, namely food, clothing, shelter, and transportation, are our basic needs. All of you children are currently dependent on your families and parents. If there is no parental support, or if parents do not pay attention, danger will arise. Therefore, you must remember that you are receiving parental support at this moment, and in the future, when you grow up, you must work hard to repay the debt of today. The second four characters, namely intelligence, physical education, morality, and aesthetics, are the four educations. Adults train your bodies, cultivate your reading, tell you the principles of being a person, and cultivate your temperament, which are the four types of education: intelligence, physical education, morality, and aesthetics. Today, in commemorating Children's Day, we must pay close attention to the profound meaning of this Double Four Day."

Li Shizeng's Speech

Li Shizeng's speech briefly stated, "The importance of children is not only in China, but also highly valued internationally. Currently, the most central international organization in the world, Geneva, has established a world school, which is entirely composed of children around the age of ten. There are currently dozens of them who are receiving global knowledge there. The school authorities have expressed their hope that Chinese children will participate in enrollment. At that time, I established a Chinese Comrades Association of the World School there to solicit Chinese children to participate. Several people have already registered. Today, I take the opportunity to propose that the Municipal Government select representatives from the children attending the meeting today to study at the World School, as a commemoration of Children's Day. On behalf of the Chinese Comrades Association of the World School, I welcome participation."

Mayor Wu giving a speech (Photo by Qichang)

Wu Xingya's Speech

Wu Xingya, Director of the Social Affairs Bureau, said briefly in his speech, "Today, commemorating Children's Day is not just for you children to come and play, but it contains great significance. China's national crisis is serious, the nation is declining, and national humiliation is increasing. To resolve the national crisis, revive the nation, and wipe out national humiliation, middle-aged and elderly people need to stand on the front lines and make sacrifices, and to continue this spirit, it all depends on you children. You children should quickly train your bodies, study hard, enrich your knowledge, not waste precious time, and strictly observe order and respect teachers, so that in the future you can avenge your ancestors, build a new China, and make it a model Three Principles of the People country in the world."

Children's Speeches

Finally, Tao Jianming, a representative of the Shangwen Elementary School children, gave a speech on [Children and the New Life Movement], and Yi Mingwang, a representative of the Fifth District Cigarette Industry Workers' Union labor children, gave a speech, briefly stating that Children's Day is to break the adult's psychology of belittling children. Now we often see many labor children living miserable and uneducated lives on the streets or in their homes. There are 800,000 workers in Shanghai, and with an average of two children per person, there are over a million ignorant children. On this Children's Day, we hope that the Municipal Government and enthusiastic gentlemen in children's affairs will promote labor children's education and seek happiness for labor children." Immediately afterwards, slogans were shouted, and the ceremony concluded.

Telegrams of Congratulations from Various Places

Yesterday, the Hong Kong Children's Celebration Association sent a telegram saying, "[Wishing all children in the country good health]." 43,242 children in Kaifeng, Henan, also telegraphed various newspapers to convey their congratulations to the children across the country, expressing their wishes.

Minister Kong's Telegram

Minister Kong Xiangxi was unable to come to Shanghai from Beijing due to official duties to participate in Children's Day and specially telegraphed Mayor Wu to deliver the following speech on his behalf: "Because there are many helpless children in our country, scattered everywhere, I gathered comrades six years ago and organized the China Child Welfare Association to implement protection, relief, hygiene, and other work, and to awaken the public's responsibility for children. With the approval of the National Government, April 4th of each year was designated as Children's Day. Today is the third anniversary, and celebrations are being held everywhere in the country to commemorate it. It is true that children are the future masters of the country. If they do not receive perfect education and nurturing during their childhood, how can they bear great responsibility in the future? Therefore, those who are responsible for promoting this cause should urgently awaken the people of the country to pay attention to children's affairs, so that everyone has the concept of loving children and bears the responsibility of loving children. At the same time, we should also make children across the country understand their own position, and strive to improve themselves in order to cultivate noble personalities. This is my original aspiration when I founded Children's Day. I hope that all comrades and children across the country will work hard."

Mayor's Reception for Children 122

Mayor's Speech

After the celebration ceremony, it rained, so the venue was changed to the Municipal Government Auditorium. Mayor Wu hosted a reception for all the children in the city. First, Mayor Wu delivered a welcoming speech, briefly stating, "Dear children, we hold a Children's Day commemorative meeting every year on April 4th, and the Municipal Government hosts a reception for children once a year, so that we can remember at all times on Children's Day that the Chinese nation has a glorious history of thousands of years and is the earliest civilized nation in the world. Therefore, we are confident that by gathering the intelligence and talent of 400 million people across the country, we can definitely revive the nation and save it from national crisis, but this responsibility must be borne by the people of the country and continue to work hard, especially since children are the lifeblood of the Chinese nation. My holding Children's Day commemoration every year is to awaken citizens to love and educate children."

Children's Reply

Next, Cao Xigang, a children's representative from Danhua Elementary School, delivered a reply, briefly stating, "Chairman, gentlemen, today we are holding a celebration for Children's Day, and we are grateful for the mayor's presentation of commemorative badges and his invitation for us to visit the various departments of the Municipal Government. The children are very grateful. Now, on behalf of all the children in the city, I would like to bow to the mayor to express our gratitude, and also to express that we have accepted the mayor's instructions."

Meeting with Representatives

The mayor then met with the children's representatives, and the mayor's wife presented gifts to the model children. The list of model children from each school is recorded below: Lin Zheng (Wusong Elementary School), Zhang Xi (Zhenxiu Elementary School), Jiang Erjing (Chongshi Elementary School), Jin Peixin (Shangwen Elementary School), Shi Huayu (Qingguang Elementary School), Wu Jintao (Jingcun Elementary School), Xu Miaogen (Mengyang Elementary School), Yang Jinggao (Mingda Elementary School), Zhu Zonglin (Zhenxi Elementary School), Zhang Ruilin (Qimei Elementary School), Lu Mingren (Zhonglu Elementary School), Xu Jiaren and Zhang Zhengqing (Boren Elementary School), Xie Pengnian (Shihua Elementary School), Meng Xiong (Minzhi Elementary School), Sun Xueqin (Peiben Elementary School), Zhang Shanqin (Zhangcun Elementary School), Ge Xingbei (Nong [blank] Elementary School), Ma Ruqian (Ai Qun Girls' Elementary), Wu Suzhen (Xun Yu Elementary School), Xie Chuyan (Hu She Elementary School), Zhang Youfeng (Songxue Elementary School), Yan Xiuzhen (Jingye Affiliated Elementary School), Yao Ruifa (Chengzhong Elementary School), Huang Shunxing (Gaochang Elementary School), Shen Zhangsheng (Huiqiao Elementary School), Peng Fengming (Haishan Elementary School), Huang Yuping (Danhua Elementary School).

The radio was also open all day, broadcasting various music and dance performances, as well as various famous people's speeches on Children's Day broadcast by the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau.

The Children’s Day Commemorative Congress, organized by the Women’s National Goods Year Movement Committee, was held at Huesha on Beijing Road at 2 pm yesterday. More than 1,000 children and parents arrived, were crowded together, and was extremely lively. The details are as follows:

Chairman's Report

The China Child Welfare Association, in view of the fact that countries around the world pay great attention to children’s affairs, specially designated a Children’s Day. Therefore, the Child Welfare Association also submitted a request to the National Government in March of the 20th year to designate April 4th as Children’s Day. So today’s celebration can also be said to be the third anniversary. All of you children are the masters of the country, and are closely related to the strength or weakness of the country. The 20th century is the century of children. If we want to save China from danger and revive the Republic of China, we must make children healthy. Therefore, today, when we celebrate Children’s Day, we should awaken the people of the country to love children, and make sure that they are fully developed physically and intellectually, especially teachers and parents who are responsible for education. As for the general poor and homeless children, we should ask the government to find ways to provide relief and shelter, so that they can all develop healthy bodies and patriotic thoughts."

(1) Mrs. Cai Yuanpei gave a speech, briefly stating that various countries have Children’s Day, but the date is different for each country. Children’s Day in China is in the late spring, which implies a thriving intention. However, when we commemorate Children’s Day here, children, do not forget the pain of the January 28th Shanghai War. There is a major significance in this, because the children of today are the masters of the future. Childhood is the budding age. It is useless without good cultivation. Therefore, the responsibility of cultivation should be on the parents and teachers. Furthermore, this congress is organized by the Women's National Goods Year Committee, so I hope that parents will provide children with national goods, so that they can be complete national goods children. The following are speeches by Pan Yangyao, Liu Wang Liming, and Yan Junxuan, etc., omitted.

Qingdao Mayor Shen Honglie Left Shanghai Yesterday 126

Yesterday Morning, Paid Respects to the War Zone

Noon, Public Banquet from the Business Community

Evening, Took the Express Train to Beijing

According to the Industrial Association, the China General Chamber of Industry, the Chinese Cotton Mill Association, various organizations, as well as Wing On Textile Company, China Tobacco Company, China Stone Company, etc., held a banquet yesterday noon at the Wing On Textile Second Factory in Wusong Yunzaobang, to welcome Qingdao Mayor Shen Honglie. The host and guest arrived together at twelve o'clock. Mayor Shen felt somewhat burdened by the receptions he had received from various circles in recent days, so no welcoming ceremony was held. The details are recorded below:

Representatives Present

Yesterday's attendees included Wang Xiaolai of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, Qian Chengxu of the China General Chamber of Industry, Zhang Zemin of the Chinese Cotton Mill Association, Guo Shun of Wing On Textile Mill, Hu Xiyuan of Asia-Pacific Electric Company, Lin Dazhong of Kaicheng Acid Manufacturing Plant, Zhang Jiongbo of China Tobacco Company, Li Yuncheng of China Gas Company, Chen Shouchang, Wang Yaochen of Fuxin Flour Company, Tao Guilin of China Stone Company, Zhu Jingan of Litai Textile Company, Zhu Gengtao of Renfeng Dyeing and Weaving Factory, and Feng Ziyuan of Shanxi Xinjiang Dayisheng Textile Company, among more than thirty others.

Guo Shun's Speech

Because no ceremony was held, the host, Guo Shun, simply delivered a welcoming speech, saying, "Two years ago, at Mayor Shen's invitation, we went to Qingdao to inspect the municipal administration. When we parted, we promised to return the visit to the South. Now, Mayor Shen has graciously fulfilled the promise before we even dared to hope for his arrival. The wise host of the past is now the honored guest of today. To gather together is truly a rare occasion. Mayor Shen studied abroad in his early years, delving into economics and political science. Upon returning to China, he made a name for himself wherever he went. In governing Qingdao, he has gradually implemented and brought to scale various projects, such as municipal engineering and harbor construction. As for the rural areas outside the city, he had not yet started. Therefore, in April of the 21st year of the Republic of China, he established construction offices in various rural districts, including Licun, Cangkou, Jiushui, Yindao, and Xuejiadao, to work closely with the people. To this day, Qingdao's municipal construction policies and rural construction plans have reached their third phase. All efforts to develop the people's livelihood, prepare for self-governance, popularize education, maintain public order, facilitate transportation, and promote agriculture, everything to transform, educate, nourish, and benefit the people, have been fully prepared. This is what we have all witnessed and heard during our recent inspection of Qingdao, and it is also the unanimous judgment of the Chinese and foreign press, repeatedly reported in the newspapers. There is no need for us to specifically promote Mayor Shen. According to Mayor Shen himself, Qingdao has become a center of domestic production with its numerous factories. However, while various circles have a strong interest in knowledge and research on industrial economics, they lack adequate understanding. Therefore, in the 22nd year of the Republic of China, he established two organizations in Qingdao. The one for research gathers domestic experts to form the Qingdao Industrial and Commercial Society, allocating substantial funding each month to support research, statistics, and investigations. The one for municipal design establishes the Qingdao Prosperity Promotion Association, hiring Mr. Chen Guangfu of Shanghai and others to synthesize its accomplishments. It is expected that within half a year, there will be significant construction discoveries. After that time, railways and shipping can be used for large-scale connections, and the foundation between the economies of Shanghai and Qingdao will also be completed. In short, Mayor Shen's only ambition and purpose is to do things practically and not engage in empty habits. We can see his inner richness today, which can be expressed in his ample style." Afterwards, Mayor Shen responded to the warm hospitality from all circles and invited everyone present to visit Qingdao before July 30th this summer and led them to Boshan and other places to inspect the glass and electrical industries in preparation for future development.

Shen's Remarks

After the banquet, Mr. Shen shared with reporters the various reasons why China's industry and commerce could not prosper: "Modern countries all base their national establishment on industry and commerce as the foundation of production. China's industrial and commercial undertakings are heading towards collapse. Is this due to lagging behind the times or oppression from the environment? In abstract terms, it is nothing more than the following points: First, entrepreneurs have unclear concepts. Modern industry and commerce do not seek short-term gains, while Chinese people seek profit from their capital. Modern industry and commerce are pragmatic, while Chinese people often rely on luck. Modern industry and commerce must understand the truth of supply and demand, while Chinese people have no statistics. Modern industry and commerce take profits as their profits, while Chinese people are selfish. Modern industry and commerce value continuous permanence, while Chinese people prefer the present. Modern industry and commerce emphasize substance, while Chinese people like to forge. Modern industry and commerce should perfect science, while Chinese people regard it as ordinary affairs. All of these are because Chinese people do not have a clear understanding of modern industry and commerce, so even with new materials, it is difficult to obtain a new spirit. Secondly, the cultivation of employees is insufficient. Modern industry and commerce value economic control, but there are not many talents who seek the overall situation. Modern industry and commerce need excellent workers, but the training of workers is insufficient. The so-called insufficient cultivation is not only in the intellectual aspect, but also in the moral aspect. In recent years, advertisements for the arrest of escaped partners, news of laziness and abandonment of work, and unexpected losses suffered by factories and shops have been frequently reported in newspapers. The old-time industrialists and merchants still knew to value trust, responsibility, frugality, diligence, endurance, and poverty. Now, they have failed to remedy the weaknesses of the old-style industry and commerce, but have first abandoned its advantages, resulting in more internal disputes, and the business is even more affected. Thirdly, the environment cannot help. The organization of modern society is intricate, and there is no relationship that is not interconnected. The expansion of one part always depends on the establishment of another part. For example, industry first emphasizes tools, and tools first emphasize hardware, so foreign countries always take the coal and iron industries as the center of industry, and the needs of coal and iron for various industries cannot be counted. If one of the components is not prepared, it is enough to change the overall situation. This is only in terms of the relationship between industrial systems. As for various undertakings other than industry and commerce, they all have a cooperative relationship with industry and commerce. For example, if education is poor, morals will be degraded and knowledge will be superficial; if politics and law are poor, life and property will lose their protection; if transportation is poor, transportation will be difficult; if agricultural products are poor, raw materials will be lacking. It is known that the industry and commerce itself and the environment of industry and commerce must be improved at the same time. Otherwise, if everyone speaks in unison, it will eventually be deteriorated by the environment. In short, if the concept is not correct, the policy will be wrong; if morality and knowledge are lacking, the undertaking will lose its basis; if the environment is scattered and not connected, the foundation will not be established. These three are the general causes of business failure, and industry and commerce are no exception."

Returned to Beijing Last Night

Yesterday morning, Mayor Shen, accompanied by Wang Xiaolai, Guo Shun, and others, went to Wusong Fort Taiwan, Yunzaobang, Zhanghuabang, and other places to visit the traces of the Songhu War. In the afternoon, Qian Chengxu, Lin Dazhong, Hu Xiyuan, and others led them to Jungong Road to visit the Kaicheng Acid Manufacturing Plant. Originally, he intended to visit the war zones in Zhabei and Jiangwan, but due to rain, he returned to the New Asia Hotel residence at about 4 p.m. He then took the night express train at 11 p.m., accompanied by staff members Guo Binghe and Liu Jingxi, and others, back to Beijing. Those who went to see him off included Wang Xiaolai, Qian Chengxu, Guo Shun, and dozens of representatives from the municipal government and others. Shen will stay in Beijing for about two days and will take a train on the morning of the 7th to return directly to Qingdao.

The Wife of U.S. Consul General Cunningham Passed Away in Hangzhou Yesterday Morning 129

Chinese and Foreign Acquaintances Mourn

Mr. Cunningham, the U.S. Consul General stationed in Shanghai, accompanied his wife by car to Hangzhou for a tour during the Easter holiday. They were originally scheduled to return to Shanghai a few days ago, but on Sunday afternoon, Mrs. Cunningham suddenly fell ill with a cold and was admitted to the China Inland Mission Hospital for treatment. Mr. Cunningham then called the Consulate General's office, saying that due to his wife's illness, they had to postpone their return to Shanghai. In addition to being treated in Hangzhou, a doctor from Shanghai was also sent to Hangzhou to diagnose and treat her. However, yesterday morning, Mr. Cunningham informed Consul Josselyn in Shanghai via long-distance telephone that his wife's condition was serious and he could not specify when they would return to Shanghai. Shortly after 11:00 a.m., another telephone call came, saying that Mrs. Cunningham had passed away. The nature of her illness remains unknown. The date of the funeral will be announced after it has been determined. Mr. and Mrs. Cunningham have been married for over twenty years. Mrs. Cunningham always accompanied Mr. Cunningham wherever he went. They first went to Mumbai, then to Singapore, then to Hankou in 1914. In November 1919, Mr. Cunningham was transferred to Shanghai. Having traveled to Shanghai for more than ten years, he has a wide circle of friends among Chinese and foreigners. Therefore, the sudden news of his wife's death has caused great grief among his acquaintances. Mrs. Cunningham was born on January 1, 1886.

The Grain and Rice Industry Re-Telegrams Guangdong, Requesting Unified Collection of Tariffs on Imported Rice 130

National Consistency is Appropriate

The Whole People Will Benefit

The Shanghai Miscellaneous Grains and Oil Cake Trade Association and the Bean and Rice Trade Association, noting that although the government has issued regulations for the collection of tariffs on imported rice, the tax rate in Guangdong Province has not yet been unified, previously telegraphed the Guangdong authorities, requesting approval for unification, in order to prevent imported rice from avoiding higher taxes and being imported from Guangdong Province in large quantities, thereby encroaching on the value of domestic rice and affecting the rural economy. One month has passed without a reply. Therefore, yesterday, they re-telegraphed Chen Jitang, reiterating their previous request. The original telegram is as follows: "In recent years, China's rural areas have collapsed, and crises are imminent. The government and the public are unanimously planning relief measures, and preventing the sale of imported rice is considered the most important measure. Guangdong Province, with its foresight, took the lead in advocating this and specially established the Bureau of Special Taxes on Imported Agricultural Products on September 16 of last year to levy import taxes on imported rice at one yuan per picul, thereby resisting the onslaught of foreign rice and seeking an outlet for the surplus grain in the Yangtze River provinces. Its grand plans are widely admired. In December, the government ordered all provinces and customs to levy new taxes on imported rice, but Guangdong Province was exempted because it had already established a special bureau. However, the tax rate in Guangdong Province is only one-third of the customs duty. As a result, foreign merchants avoid the heavier taxes and, having failed in other provinces, flock to Guangdong, taking advantage of the loopholes to enter in a steady stream. According to statistics, in January and February of this year, there were as many as sixteen ships carrying imported rice into Guangdong Province, and the same is likely true in March. If the loopholes are not plugged, the overall effect will not be seen. Is this the original intention of Guangdong Province to establish a bureau to levy taxes and relieve the rural areas? Therefore, this association telegraphed the Southwest Political Affairs Committee and the Guangdong Provincial Government in February, requesting approval for a unified tax rate. The Political Affairs Committee replied that it would await the provincial government's review and decision. However, for a month, the Chinese people have been waiting with anticipation, hoping for good news from the south, but no decree has been issued, causing deep anxiety. Today, the great powers are pursuing their dumping policies, seeking world markets. China, with its backward industry, is well-suited to supply them. The excess of industrial products has already damaged our rights, and the invasion of agricultural products has shaken the foundations of the country. Therefore, raising tariffs to strengthen our defenses should be done consistently across the country. Now, because one side of the net is still sparse and the success of nine mountains has not been completed, the rice-producing areas in the Yangtze River region are sitting idle, unsold, and the price is trending even lower, causing the people to suffer even more. If Guangdong Province unifies the tax rate and jointly implements preventative measures, the people in Guangdong will abandon imported rice and choose domestic rice, without any losses. Domestic rice will be unhindered, benefiting the entire population. Mutual assistance is valued in both ancient and modern times. We have always admired Guangdong Province as the source of revolutionary strategies, and the patriotic people and caring authorities will surely consider the overall situation and be happy to promote it. Therefore, we reiterate our heartfelt request and urge you to immediately inform the Guangdong Provincial Government to increase the tariff on imported rice in accordance with the current import tariff rate. We await your orders with trepidation. Respectfully, Gu Xinyi, Chairman of the Shanghai Miscellaneous Grains and Oil Cake Trade Association and the Bean and Rice Trade Association."
