Shen Bao National Goods Weekly

Words of Contribution

Welcome to Mayor Shen, a Enthusiastic Supporter of National Goods 195

— Yang Yan

Mayor Shen Honglie of Qingdao is traveling south to inspect construction, education, and the national goods industry. He is passing through Shanghai, and the Municipal Chamber of Commerce and various national goods organizations warmly welcome him to discuss cooperation between the two cities' industrial and commercial enterprises. The reporter also followed the comrades in the national goods industry to visit Qingdao and greatly admired Mayor Shen's concern for the development of the national goods industry, taking the prosperity of Qingdao as his mission. Last summer, the Qingdao National Goods Exhibition was opened under the leadership of Mayor Shen. Its business development broke the unprecedented record of various provinces and cities. We also personally listened to Mayor Shen's sincere advocacy of national goods, which inspired the leaders of the Shanghai and Qingdao national goods industries to organize businesses. Qingdi Ding Jingchen, Liu Zishan, and Wang Xin pioneered the Qingdao National Goods Company. At the same time, Fang Yixian, Cai Shengbai, Ren Shigang, Fang Jiange, and Li Zumo Xu Yangnan jointly established the Shandong United Sales Office of National Goods Factories. They all received Mayor Shen's support, which led to their success today. Therefore, not only the Qingdao business community is grateful for his enthusiasm, but also the Shanghai national goods community admires his good intentions. This is most welcome. Wang Xiaolai said, "Today, Shanghai merchants who regard Qingdao as a sales area should take a step further and regard Qingdao as an investment area." The reporter completely agrees with this statement and sincerely hopes that this summer, our national goods community and financial community will revisit Qingdao to seek the construction of the national goods industry, with Qingdao as an investment area for the financial and national goods community, to "curb the Japanese invasion and develop Qingdao's resources." This is what we especially hope for.

The Spring Season of the "Women's National Goods Year" 196

— Xuan Wan

"The planning for the year lies in the spring," the ancients have clearly told us that the progress of any career must be based on a well-defined plan in the spring, and then in this year, we can follow this fixed procedure, continue to work hard, and reach the final goal. Naturally, although these are only a few words, they are a good mirror for the progress of our national goods industry.

We deeply know that in the past history, the soaring slogan of advocating national goods has now entered its second year - from the National Goods Year to the Women's National Goods Year. In this short process, because of our efforts, it has already achieved considerable results. As the cause indicates, we can take Nanjing Road, which is usually full of foreign goods, as an example. Previously, it was the base camp for imported goods, but now it has five or six national goods shopping malls, especially the China National Goods Company, which is the most complete and largest, becoming the "General Warehouse of National Goods," loved and supported by the public. In addition, the North National Goods Shopping Mall hosted by the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, and yesterday, we heard that the South National Goods Shopping Mall has also opened. How great! Good news for national goods. All these things give us a good impression. However, on the other hand, last year's "new record of 900 million yuan in import surplus" and this time, "the United States raised silver prices, attempting to dump goods," makes us feel that the foundation we have established in the past is not enough, and it is necessary to expand the future. Now, I dare to put forward two sincere hopes, based on my personal opinions, and contribute them to the authorities in charge of our national goods industry, so that they can plan and implement them as soon as possible.

(1) Establish national goods companies in various places. Mr. Pan Yangyao proposed a list of national goods companies to be established in various places in the previous issues of this journal, and detailed their total turnover and capital amount. How can we make them all come true in the shortest period of time, so as to form a national network of national goods, so that the enthusiastic call for advocating national goods is not only limited to a corner of the city, but also universally promoted to the inland - to all the rural areas.

(2) Determine the organization of national goods in this city. Although there are already many national goods sales organizations in Shanghai, it is necessary to reasonably regulate their business scope and region, in order to achieve more "twice the result with half the effort." Of course, we should pay attention to both not gathering in one place and facilitating residents to purchase nearby. Our future goal should be to continue to establish them in Hongkou, Zhabei, and western Shanghai, as they are suitable for the above two principles.

At this beautiful spring time, it is the time for us to devote ourselves to our careers. What's more, advocating national goods is our bounden duty and cannot be shirked. How will we embrace our mission, recognize our responsibility, and make a reasonable plan as soon as possible, and work hard to move forward, so as to be comparable to the Soviet Union's five-year plan, and achieve the greatest effect in this "Women's National Goods Year."

What are the Reasons for the Failure of the National Goods Movement? 197

— Yang Yun

No matter what kind of movement, it is inevitable to use the power of propaganda as a starting point. However, under the great propaganda, the number of people in the society who respond naturally increases day by day. Then, there should be a systematic, realistic, and detailed content method made public so that this movement can move forward in an orderly manner when it is implemented and can really take effect. The movement itself will become stronger and more powerful: otherwise, although the propaganda effect is great, and there are many responses, it feels empty and difficult to find a real way to do it. Those who are interested feel hesitant and depressed: those who are perfunctory are willing to follow blindly and deceive each other. As a result, either a form is left in the society, or even the form is difficult to maintain, and the movement is ultimately ineffective.

Our national goods movement, although it did not start today, can be said to be at its peak today. What national goods year, women's national goods year, what lectures, parades, etc., have done a lot of propaganda work as a starting point. This may not be a good phenomenon, but because there are few practical and concrete measures in terms of implementation, the result of the movement has been that the import surplus has increased from 500 million yuan to 700 million yuan, which greatly disappoints us. Therefore, I personally hope that the national goods industry will pay attention to practical measures in the future in order to achieve the actual effect of the movement.

What kind of measures are considered practical and effective? This is a question that is difficult to answer in one word. I am not talented, and I can only briefly describe its principles. What are the principles?

(1) The government must have the determination to promote national goods and save profits. All orders for the national goods movement should be strictly investigated to see if the people are following them? Strict rewards and punishments should be given, and it should not be considered that the responsibility is completed with a mere document.

(2) Leaders from all walks of life should assist the government in investigating the performance of the people's compliance and report to the government at any time. They should also set an example in themselves.

(3) All sectors of industry and commerce should have mutual supervision and eliminate the evil nature of colluding with each other.

(4) In terms of civilian clothing, the first step is for education authorities in various places to fulfill the responsibility of guidance; the second step is for special investigation authorities in various counties and districts to conduct thorough investigations to determine punishment.

The Necessary Understanding of National Goods 198

— Wu Yafei

Advocating national goods is not useful by simply shouting slogans and posting slogans; nor is it considered to have fulfilled the responsibility by following everyone and shouting a few times "National Goods Year" and "Women's National Goods Year." In fact, we don't need this kind of empty verbal ornament - a nice-sounding term. We should all stand up and do it practically, to do the patriotic work that we should do; the first step of patriotic work should be to advocate national goods.

Since the wave of the global economic downturn entered China, our national finances have also been exhausted to this point; the bankruptcy of commercial markets and the collapse of the rural economy have in fact put China's future in a period of turmoil. In particular, the stagnation of the national goods industry; on the one hand, it is subjected to the economic invasion of foreign goods, and on the other hand, it is reduced by the purchase of the people, and it has been subjected to these two pressures invisibly. As a result, the national goods industry has plummeted and become unbearable.

Moreover, the people of our country have always had a heavy mentality of favoring imported goods, so the general modern fashionable figures, whether male or female, are all advocating foreignization in their clothing, food, housing, and transportation. According to the surveys obtained from all aspects, compared with the foreign goods imported by our country every year, its number is really astonishing!

We don't talk about saving the country, just let people say "cold-blooded animals" and "reserve troops for the slaves of the country." If we want to talk about saving the country, we must first love the country; the way to love the country is to advocate national goods and boycott foreign goods. However, if we want to advocate national goods, we must first recognize our position, hold on to our purpose, and at least have a deep understanding of the content of national goods. This is definitely not to show off and just shout on the mouth. Like this kind of incomplete and hypocritical concept, we should first eliminate it, otherwise the effect is equal to zero; because this is a great barrier to the promotion of national goods.

Originally, the responsibility of advocating national goods should be shared by all citizens; the so-called "the rise and fall of the country is the responsibility of every man," is also the reason. I hope that those fashionable friends and modern women who love to use foreign goods will not be so obsessed with foreign goods, and quickly take a sense of conscience to love the country!

Finally, I myself am determined to adopt national goods for everything within the scope possible; (1) do not say that foreign goods are good, (2) do not say that national goods are bad, (3) encourage my family and children to love and use national goods, (4) persuade my relatives and friends to promote national goods, (5) as long as I think they are satisfactory, I will use them. At the same time, I only hope that our countrymen will also have a deep understanding of national goods and promote them as much as possible.

Promoting National Goods and the New Life Movement 199

— Zhang Mengzhao

The New Life Movement of etiquette, righteousness, integrity, and shame is so brilliant! Since it started in Nanchang, it has spread throughout the country, but how can we talk about etiquette, righteousness, integrity, and shame if we don't live a frugal life and tighten our degree of life?

To live a frugal life, we should first promote national goods, and start by purchasing and using national goods! In the New Life Covenant, in terms of clothing, item 9 "Clothes should be made of national goods," which is also implementing the New Life without forgetting national goods!

Confucius once said: "Do not look at what is contrary to propriety, do not listen to what is contrary to propriety, do not speak what is contrary to propriety, and do not move what is contrary to propriety." Now, Eastern, Western, and foreign goods are like charming women - fox spirits - sucking blood and cream, making a good China thin and emaciated. After implementing the New Life, I hope that the people of the country will not look at, listen to, speak of, or move non-national goods. This is "etiquette"!

"Sacrifice one's life for righteousness" and "righteousness cannot be agreed with." We should promote national goods, sparing no effort, and we cannot shirk our responsibility. Everyone should embrace the idea of being alone when everyone is drunk, and righteousness cannot be agreed with. The so-called "honesty and integrity in business" sells national goods, uses national goods, and believes in national goods. This is "righteousness"!

"Thriftiness to cultivate integrity" and "strictness and integrity in public service" are virtues that everyone should have! It is better to be frugal and purchase national goods, and cultivate the foundation of the country with integrity, so as not to allow the outflow of interests, which can be called "integrity"!

"Know shame and teach war" and "knowing shame is close to courage." But the country is not competitive and has suffered heavy shame, and has no ability to fight externally! Knowing shame and being brave in civil war, and being brave in buying enemy goods is really heartbreaking! There are also those shameless merchants who recognize thieves as fathers and use the money of their compatriots to seek the destruction of their own motherland. They are full of evil and their crimes are heinous! Dear compatriots, if we do not eliminate the traitors and exclude the imported goods from the East and the West, the shame will lead to economic destruction of the country, the destruction of the family, and the death of the people! Therefore, "know shame" and quickly use national goods! "Ming shame" quickly plan to deal with traitors, and deal with our enemies, and be ashamed to buy enemy goods! Be ashamed to be in the company of traitors! This is knowing "shame"! To sum up, the four words "etiquette, righteousness, integrity, and shame" should be started from one's own position by "promoting national goods"!

The Mission of Female Teachers in the Women's National Goods Year 200

— Youzhi

The object of education is students, and those who bear this educational responsibility are teachers. The words and deeds of teachers directly affect students and indirectly affect the entire society, because education is inseparable from society, guiding society on the one hand and improving society on the other. Therefore, we believe that teachers are in a position to lead the masses, not only to set an example for children, but also to further and practically serve as mentors to the masses. Only in this way can we achieve the long-term goals of education, and only then can teachers fulfill their responsibilities!

In the booming advocacy of national goods, although it requires the concerted efforts of the people of the country, the responsibilities of teachers are not small. On the one hand, they must publicize the significance of the national goods movement, and on the other hand, they must thoroughly transform the bad habit of loving to use foreign goods. Teachers can also be said to be people who are deeply rooted in the people, so it is of course easier to get started, and the results will be great in the future!

This year is the Women's National Goods Year, so of course it focuses on the women's national goods movement, which shows that in the past, women used a lot of foreign goods, and now they want to make a big turn in the right direction - adopting national goods. This is really a great project! What kind of efforts do women across the country need to make in order to achieve this: Of course, female teachers must take on even greater missions! This is undeniable! Women's education in China has not reached a considerable stage, and the level of knowledge is childish, which is a general phenomenon. And female teachers are intellectuals, and can be said to be outstanding among the common people. It is most suitable for them to be in a position to lead their female compatriots, and they can really be role models for the women's community! Therefore, we believe that female teachers are the pioneers of the Women's National Goods Year. If they can recognize their own position and set an example, the future of the women's national goods movement will be full of unlimited light!

If the minds of female teachers are only filled with foreignization, fabrics, decorations, and daily necessities, and they only seek foreign goods, this is the "foreign-style education" that has harmed them, which is tantamount to a policy of suicide and self-destruction! Not only is it of no benefit to society and the country, but it is also a scourge! I can give an example. There is a female teacher in a rural primary school, who can be considered to have a good relationship with the local area. Ordinary rural women often accompany her and are gradually influenced by the female teacher. Their hair is cut, their faces are painted with snow cream, and their clothes are made of foreign cloth cheongsams. In this way, they seem to have changed their faces and have completely turned into modern girls. I feel that the power of this female teacher is really great, and maybe in the near future, those village girls will paint their eyebrows, apply rouge, and wear high heels like this female teacher! Naturally, there are good and bad points here, but after all, the bad points outweigh the good points several times! The female teacher has simply become a model salesperson for foreign goods! It is reasonable to say that they should not have fallen from the supreme and noble position to the miserable situation of being lowly and declining:

To put it another way: teachers are called teachers because they can teach children. Children's psychology is malleable, and we must cultivate them to develop good habits so that they can devote themselves to the country and become good citizens in the future. If they have been trained to maturity, there is no need to have a national goods movement when they become adults! And aren't the students taught by female teachers following this common goal! Shouldn't that be advocating national goods?

Spring and Autumn

Records of Drifting Fragrance 202

— Translated by Qin Shouou

(1) Golden Sands Everywhere

In the spring, peach blossoms are blooming everywhere inside and outside the city of Beiping, as if competing for beauty; when a gust of wind passes, fallen flowers cover the ground, as if laying a crimson carpet; in the air, you can smell the strong fragrance of other flowers at any time.

On a certain street, the ground is covered with golden sand, and a large group of people and horses are advancing mightily. The ranks are extremely neat and solemn. Except for the light and crisp rustling sound of people and horses trampling on the sand, nothing else can be heard.

Many people in splendid costumes, riding horses and wearing朝 hats decorated with sable tails, form a brilliant team. The horses under them are all of the best Mongolian breed, with smooth fur and long, neat tails, which often emit dazzling light. The saddles are inlaid with precious jewels, and the stirrups also have very beautiful decorations. On average, each horse has at least four or five different colors. Hundreds of horses gathered together, coupled with the reflection of the sun, make it a spectacular sight, as bright as clouds!

Behind the dust raised by these horses, about ten or twenty steps apart, is a large, foldable sedan chair that shines with the brilliance of gold. On both sides of the sedan chair are painted two golden dragons with bared teeth and claws. Sixteen eunuchs are carrying the sedan chair. Inside this sedan chair, sitting as still as a deity in a temple, is the Empress Dowager Cixi of the time, the ruler of China's 400 million people. (3)

Spring and Autumn

Wu Palace Flowers and Grass 203

— Yan Qiao

The Suzhou flower market can be described as [renowned since ancient times]. If you take a rickshaw, you can see many flower sheds at Tiger Hill and Shantang, covered with reed curtains on top and flowers hidden underneath. When the weather is sunny and the air is mild, and the curtains are rolled up to reveal the flowers, although you can't smell the fragrance, it seems to waft into the carriage.

Also, when staying at a hostel near Adai Bridge, in the early morning, you often see groups of women carrying bamboo baskets selling white orchid flowers, disturbing your peaceful dreams and arousing your idle sentiments. This also shows that the Suzhou flower market [is still thriving].

Speaking of plum blossoms, Dengwei Mountain is naturally the most well-established. The phrase "Fragrant Snow Sea" often lingers in people's minds. However, in recent years, due to the limited production of plums, many have been replaced with mulberry trees. It's truly a transformation from sea to mulberry field, far inferior to the prosperity of Wuxi. Zhang's Garden, a rising star, still has much to offer. In addition, Lengxiang Pavilion, although having a small amount, is merely a dependent state, a situation of partial peace.

There is a plum blossom tree in Li Yin's old home, which came from Anhui. The trunk is seven or eight inches in circumference, leaning as if drunk, with flower branches slanting out from the top, like hair fluttering in the wind, scattered with fragrance, intoxicating people. Mr. Xu Yunqiu happened to be present and took out a photograph from his side to show me. The scene was similar, but more twisted and coiled, appearing even more ancient. He said it was a relic of the famous painter Gu Heyi. When Heyi was alive, a Japanese painter saw it and offered five hundred taels of silver to buy it. Heyi refused, and the Japanese painter took a photograph and included it in his travelogue, saying that it was at least a hundred years old.

This year, the magnolia flowers in my home are blooming exceptionally well, totaling about five hundred. The gentle breeze shakes the white blossoms, and the warm sun reflects the light. It truly feels solemn and brilliant. If described in Western words, calling it sacred would be most fitting.

These days, when the carriage passes through the south of the city, most of the new buildings are decorated with a few flowering trees, with pink and red blossoms peeking out from the low walls, reminding one of the poem [Spring colors fill the garden, unable to be confined], truly feeling that flowers are the daughters of the era.

The Impact of Undermining Modernity 204

— Tianxu Wo Sheng

According to reports, a strange group [undermining modernity] has been discovered in Hangzhou. It is now the Qingming Festival season, and Hangzhou's commerce has always relied on the spring and autumn outings for a large portion of its income. In the past, due to floods, the tide-watching was canceled. According to people in the business community, each store in the city made five million less in business. This shows that Fan Wenzheng's governance of Hangzhou, allowing people to compete in dragon boat races, and monks and Taoists building temples and monasteries, allowed people with surplus money to spend it, and those with skills could earn money by using their strength. It was truly a wonderful strategy for relieving unemployment and regulating finance. If modern figures were to regard Hangzhou as a dangerous place and stop visiting, it would affect the city's commerce and become a suicidal policy for the people of Hangzhou. In fact, rayon has taken the place of silk, and wool has taken the sales of silk and cotton, not in the form of modern or not modern. Then, glamorous attire and Western clothing are still just forms. If domestic silk is used for glamorous attire and Western clothing, I don't think it will be ruined by strong water.

Because someone asked me if Hangzhou is safe to visit, I said that it definitely won't ruin your clothes. However, when foreigners come to China to preach, they even change to wear our Chinese clothing. We are not going to foreign countries to be foreign slaves, so why do we need to change to wear Western clothing?

Four Company Commanders of the Northeast 205

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter Twenty-Six: Generously Baring His Heart, Forgetting Family and Serving the Nation; Sadly Facing the Jade Mirror, Sighing for My Yearning Heart

Gui Zhi nodded slightly, without saying a word. Ms. Jiang said: "Go to sleep, don't think about anything." Gui Zhi was also afraid that her mother would worry, so she nodded and said in a low voice: "I'm going to sleep now. It's cold tonight." As she spoke, she reached out to unbutton her clothes. Moreover, with drowsy eyes, she even yawned twice, indicating that she was absolutely going to sleep. Seeing her in this state, Ms. Jiang naturally didn't say anything more, closed the door for her and quietly left. Gui Zhi closed the door, walked to the table, and also wanted to move the lamp and go to bed. Because there was a mirror next to the lamp, she thought, "Do I have a sad look on my face? Why would my mother see through my thoughts?" So she sat down again, held the mirror with both hands, and looked at her face closely in the light. This time, she finally saw her face clearly. Her eyes, from the outside to the inside, were all red, and her round cheeks now had two prominent cheekbones. They were definitely not like the skin of a water chestnut and the color of peach petals when she was a bride. Looking at her own reflection, and then looking up at the photograph hanging on the wall, she couldn't help but sigh. Suddenly, Ms. Jiang said outside the window: "Young lady, you said you were going to sleep, why aren't you sleeping yet?" Then Zhao Weng also said: "Yes, the weather is quite cold, don't catch a cold." Gui Zhi then understood that the two old people hadn't slept yet, so she replied: "I'm going to sleep now, I'm going to sleep now." She answered and actually went to bed to sleep. But not wanting to sleep, yet forcing herself to sleep, made it even harder to fall asleep. As a result, she lay on the pillow and thought even more wildly. This night's fantasies planted countless seeds of sorrow in Gui Zhi, and the future changes were something that Gui Zhi herself could not have imagined. (354)

Miscellaneous Talk

Research on Inkstones (16) 208

— Bored Guest

General Situation of She Inkstones

(1) Assessment and Discussion of She and Duan Inkstones

She inkstones are produced on Longwei Mountain in Wuyuan, Huizhou. According to Xin'an Zhi, during the Kaiyuan period of the Tang Dynasty, a hunter named Ye chased a beast to the Great Wall and saw叠stones that were crystal clear. He brought them back and made inkstones. They were warmer and more moist than Duanxi inkstones. He held them to the command and presented them. During the reign of Emperor Yuanzong of the Southern Tang Dynasty, the governor of She presented the stone to the court and recommended the inkstone craftsman Li Shaowei, who was promoted to inkstone official. The name of She inkstone became famous from then on. The Inkstone Manual also says that the Chengxintang paper used by Li Houzhu, the Li Tinggui ink, and the Longwei stone inkstone were the best in the world. It is a beautiful story passed down in history. At that time, Duanxi inkstones were not yet famous, so commentators only praised She. Later, the mining of the Lower Rock stone of Duanxi gradually increased, and the number of people praising the Lower Rock of Duanxi increased. As a result, inkstone commentators were divided into two factions, one saying that the firmness and inking ability of She stone was better than Duan, and the other saying that the warmth, fineness and density of Duan stone was better than She. Each held one view. We can fairly say that both have their merits. The Relics of the Inkstone Forest says: "Longwei is like a clear and cold Taoist, often seeing opportunities; Duan stone is like a romantic scholar, with a bright and smooth body." This theory is the most fair. Ouyang Xiu and Su Dongpo both loved and valued this product, because the Longwei of She and the North Wall stone of Duan are as moist and greasy as melted wax. Unfortunately, the old pits of Longwei were abandoned as early as the Northern Song Dynasty. The new pits that have been produced since then are not as good as the old pits. The Lower Rock of Duanxi has become more and more refined, and the new pits are better than the old pits. This is why Duan stone has created its unique position.

(2) She Stones are divided into five grades. According to Tang Hengquan's "Theory of Inkstones," She inkstones are divided into five categories, all of which are generally firm, smooth, and good for inking, with those with gold stars that are clearly visible and bright, and as brilliant as gold paint, being the most valuable. The best ones have a shape like a dragon's tail and are called Dragon Tail Gold Stars. The next best are those with gold stars scattered like fallen flower petals. All those with gold stars must have a greenish stone color. In addition to the gold stars, there are other patterns like reed flowers, or like woven silk, or like eyebrows, or like brushed silk; the patterns are all white, faintly like silver. These four types are the next best (but the good ones are also very rare). As for the stone without patterns, it is not all ordinary stone. There is a kind of stone with a slightly rough texture, which feels sharp to the touch, so it is very good for inking, and is also a good one. The above is a distinction based on stone grade.

(3) Old Pits and New Pits, Inkstone Theory also calls the Longwei Old Pit, which is also a cobblestone that is difficult to find in large sizes. The color is light blue-black, clear as autumn water, and has no patterns. When immersed in water, it seems slightly purple, and it is as fine and smooth as jade, or faintly has white patterns, forming mountains and rivers, ink cattle, stars, moon, and other different images. When dry, it is hidden, and when inking, it is like oil, silent, and the edge does not fade after long use. Or there are those that are pure black like horns, which are valuable. The old pits in the Southern Tang Dynasty had them, but they no longer exist now. The new pit also has a blue-black color without patterns, and it is dry, abrasive, and the ink fades. After a long time, it becomes dull and lacking. The other old pit grades such as Luowen are all blue-black in color, and their value is not reduced from Longwei. If the new pit's four grades are drier than the old pit, and the patterns are also coarser. It also says: The gold stars of the new and old pits are both coarse and dry, and the color is also light blue-black. The places with stars are not suitable for grinding ink, and workers often take it from the side, and place the stars on the outside, calling it the gold star wall. The silver stars of the new and old pits (the surface has many white dots like millet, which are silver stars) are also light blue-black, and coarse and dry like gold stars. The above is a distinction based on new and old pits.

Young men and women, distinguished guests, but when you have slipped away from the age of youth, removed the beautiful decorations, there are not many young men and women distinguished guests to come into your arms!

I sighed softly at the lonely ferry. The iron chains of the crane were still rumbling on the dock. The muffled shouts of the coolies, and the songs of the home-sick sailors, played a Volga boatmen's song together.

Yarn and Cotton 226

Yarn Stocks in Warehouses Increase Daily

Totaling 36,155 bales at the end of March.

The amount of yarn stored in the warehouses of the Shanghai Yarn Exchange is increasing daily as factories release their inventory, putting significant pressure on the market. As a result, market prices have fallen sharply recently. Spot yarn prices in April reached a new low since 19(Illegible Character), reaching 167.9 yuan, a decrease of 17.1 yuan compared to the highest price of 185 yuan on March 15th. Spot cotton prices in April were 42.3 yuan, a decrease of only 1.5 yuan. A comparison of the two reveals the difficulties faced by the factories. Xin Shen Factory, aware of the hardship caused by cheap yarn and expensive cotton, once considered purchasing and convening factories to unite and maintain prices. However, each factory only cared about their immediate interests and continued to release their yarn into warehouses. Consequently, Xin Shen Factory, seeing the unfavorable situation, painfully liquidated all 40,000 bales. This is the origin of the rumor spread by Japanese merchants. As of March 31st, the total was 36,155 bales. The breakdown is listed below:

Spot Market Closed for Spring Holiday

Spot Yarn and Cotton Sales Remain Sluggish

The yarn market closed for the Spring Holiday. Spot cotton yarn merchants gathered in the market, but transactions remained sporadic. No group had a significant appetite, so market sentiment was calm. However, the US and Indian cotton markets rose slightly, but this did not stimulate sales, due to tight credit conditions. The total amount purchased by all groups for the day was only 106 bales. There was no afternoon market. The amounts purchased by each group were as follows:

Inland 35 Guangdong 50 Nanyang 5

Fujian 4 Ningbo 2 Jiangxi 10

The cotton market remained dull, and market sentiment was scattered. However, US and Indian cotton prices rose, while the yarn market in this city declined, causing difficulties for the factories. Imports of raw materials were slow, leading to an increasingly sluggish market.

US Cotton Initially Fell but Ultimately Rose

Yesterday's US cotton market initially fell due to foreign merchants selling, but later rose due to short covering and a strong rebound on Wall Street. As a result, spot prices rose 5 points and futures prices rose 1 to 7 points. Liverpool spot cotton rose 6 points and futures fell 3 points. Egyptian spot cotton rose 3 points. The Bombay cotton market rose due to European exporters selling July futures. As a result, Pingal rose 3 rupees, Oomra rose 1 rupee 75 cents, and White Rocks rose 4 rupees. Grain River Down Rice Market Remains Stable 227

(Shanghai South) Over 40 groups arrived (over 6,000 piculs). Initially, the market was slightly firm with sellers calling for higher prices due to the cloudy weather. Then, drizzling rain tightened the situation. However, the changing clouds made it difficult to predict, and the brief improvement quickly vanished, turning into a slight decline. Although purchases by the Nanyang group ceased, the Northern Ports group purchased 2,450 bags of Qingjiao, Songsi, and Xilian late rice varieties, and prices remained relatively stable. Regular Bang Su Tong and Nangang thick glutinous rice varieties showed a pattern of strong initial demand followed by a decline in urban and rural stores, and prices remained normal and similar to before. The price of Du Yangjian remained the same due to balanced supply and demand, and Yin Yuan remained average.

(Shanghai North) Yesterday, over 20 vessels arrived from the river ports, and sales were limited due to the rain in the early morning. Most merchants did not open their scales, and the market remained firm.

Guest Xian Rice Merchants Offer Limited Price Sales 228

Mid-Grade Xian Rice Continues to Rise by 5 Cents

Yesterday, the Guest Xian rice market continued to show good prospects. Due to high production costs, merchants received price limits from the producing areas and were unwilling to sell easily. All higher-grade rice varieties were offered at prices 20 cents higher, but buyers considered the prices too high and did not inquire. Mid-grade varieties had more stock, with new arrivals from various locations along the Yangtze River and north of the Yangtze. The market price could not be increased significantly. Yesterday, due to the activity of (Illegible Character) merchants, prices also rose by 5-6 cents. However, local merchants and Han merchants in this city directly chartered a shallow-water vessel in Changsha, fully loaded with Hunan rice, and shipped it directly from Hunan to Shanghai, expected to arrive in Shanghai soon. Therefore, merchants were not as optimistic about mid-grade Xian rice as they were about higher-grade varieties. A total of 5,588 bags were sold, with 224 bags going to Wenzhou, 400 bags going to this street, and the rest going to Fuzhou from the Min province group.

Yellow Soybean Sales Less Active Than Before 229

Yesterday, the yellow soybean market was less active than the previous day. Only factories were purchasing, with no other inquiries. Factories purchased 1,800 bags of Guide soybeans at a price of 2.6 yuan, 1,200 bags of Dangshan soybeans at a price of 2.58 to 2.55 yuan, and 500 bags of Xuzhou soybeans at a price of 2.5 yuan. The market price was adjusted down by 2-3 cents. No train carloads of soybeans were opened. The future trend is likely to remain flat and sluggish.

Sugar Market Coarse and White Sugar Prices Rise by 5 Cents

Yesterday, the sugar market trend was slightly better, but imports and exports were still not smooth. The association set the price of ordinary coarse white sugar at 19.85 yuan, an increase of 5 cents from the previous day. Stock in this godown was 19.95 yuan, with unchanged original prices for 89 number Ho Red sugar. Taikoo Sugar B (Illegible Character) remained at 20.25 yuan, standing firm. Zhen Ji Number One factory's fine white sugar was 18.4 yuan, with few transactions at the quoted price. Only over 100 bags of Shi Long red sugar were offered at a price of 13.5 yuan, and 60 bags of Lei Dan red sugar were offered at a price of 13.3 yuan. The Chao Qing market remained stable without further offers. Merchants were not eager to import due to low sales, resulting in a lack of transactions. It was reported that white slab sugar from Hong Kong would be shipped to Shanghai. This type of sugar has never been imported before and is being tested in the market. Samples were discussed with merchants yesterday, but the selling price has not yet been determined.

North-South Goods and Orchid Bamboo Branches Market Is Dull 230

The orchid bamboo branches produced in Zhangzhou experienced a small number of transactions in the middle of last month, and the market showed a slight upward trend. However, sales soon became sluggish again, causing the market price to decline again. It was found that the Fair Wheel imported only 40 boxes from Xiamen the day before. Although the number of arrivals was small, sales were also low, making it difficult to change the situation. It was heard that there was also little stock on the ground, and the purchase price had increased instead, creating a situation of upside-down prices. The market was exceptionally dull.

Silk and Tea Zhejiang Construction Department Keenly Improving Silk 231

(Hang Shao Agriculture, Sericulture, and Hatchery Improvement Seeds) The Zhejiang Construction Department is keenly improving silk, organizing a Silk Improvement Committee, notifying all counties about agricultural, sericultural, and hatchery improvement seeds, issuing prohibitions on the sale of native breeds, as the Qingming Festival approaches, early silkworm farmers are about to release silkworm eggs, and late silkworm farmers have already hatched them. This year, farmers in Linping, Yuhang, Changan, Haiyan, and other places are all hatching improved breeds. It is regrettable that due to low prices last year, the number of eggs hatched is not smooth, and native breeds have been eliminated. Recently, the weather has been unfavorable, with overcast rain and cold, which has been unfavorable for hatching. Therefore, the silkworm eggs of early silkworms are emerging unevenly. As the peak hatching season arrives, the weather is gradually turning sunny and warm, and agricultural sericulture is now progressing smoothly.

(Thirty Bales of Doupion Silk Shipped to Bombay) The demand for doupion silk in India remains strong, while Shanghai's inventory is limited. The British ship that arrived the day before yesterday only exported thirty bales of doupion silk, destined for Bombay.

(Yellow and White Filature Silk Sales to Europe Remain Sluggish) The overseas raw silk market was closed for three days due to Christmas. No telegrams arrived in Shanghai from New York. Although there was some trading of white filature silk in London, the incoming prices remained low, and actual sales in Lyon were stagnant. Market sentiment remained sluggish, and a turnaround in silk sales is unlikely in the short term. Yesterday, only eight bales of yellow silk were imported by Bo Hing and other companies, and prices remained depressed.

Piece Goods Japanese Woolen Fabrics Deadline for Clearance Sale 232

Imports of Japanese woolen fabrics have increased sharply, and sales have been particularly strong. Sales by customers from Sichuan, Tianjin, Changsha, and local streets have become even more active. Among industry operators, those dealing in Japanese goods account for sixty to seventy percent, and Western goods and other goods have been greatly affected. Therefore, it was resolved in the public meeting to sell all Japanese goods before the middle of this month, after which sales will be suspended. As a result, the selling price of Japanese goods has seen a drop, such as retail sales in stores falling considerably. However, non-member stores and customers are still secretly trading. The guild is currently planning measures to address this.

Free Talk

Talking About Ghosts 233

— Shan Zhi

Recently, folklorists have researched that superstitions about ghosts and gods are not entirely psychological, but mostly caused by the material environment. Life in the north is difficult, with severe winters and hot summers, so people cannot help but emphasize material things. The natural environment in the south is better, which allows for leisure in life, so the spirit can be more active. A class of sorcerers has emerged in society, specializing in making trouble among people. Wu and Chu have had many licentious sacrifices since ancient times.

However, a few charitable halls or Tongshan Societies cannot promote people's superstitions if people do not need ghosts and gods or if superstitions do not have a traditional foundation. China is a [theocracy], and ghosts and gods originally had objective material functions, not subjective spiritual responses or supernatural powers.

What is the reason for this? Generally speaking, a group of people live unsatisfactorily, have nowhere to express their feelings, and have nowhere to appeal their grievances. [They cannot afford to file a lawsuit], so they can only resent heaven and earth and pray to ghosts and gods, taking the other party to the City God Temple to ask the Bodhisattva to judge. The [oaths] of ancient times were like this!

Good must be rewarded, evil must be punished, either extending life for several decades or bringing disaster to descendants. These theories of cause and effect may be valuable to this nation and are all attached to ghosts and gods. However, [in a well-governed world, its ghosts are not divine]. The creation of ghosts and gods mostly occurs in times of turmoil. Many people think that the prevalence of Buddhism in recent years is a phenomenon of [people thinking about harmony], but they do not know that this is a manifestation of [people thinking about chaos]. The situation is not peaceful, people have lost their self-confidence, have no joy in life, and in desperation, can only hope for other lives, Pure Land, and heaven, and seek help from the ghosts and gods in the dark.

Just imagine, how many out of 400 million people are not afraid of ghosts? How common are ancestral halls and temples everywhere! Especially like the modern times of the Spring and Autumn Period and the Northern and Southern Dynasties, how can ox gods and snake ghosts not come out to stroll around [the big world] and relax! Of course, this is an era of great achievement for ghosts and gods. The ancients [laid down the butcher knife and became a Buddha on the spot]; today's people [lay down the Buddhist scriptures and pick up the butcher knife again]. Warlords and bandits bow their heads when they enter the temple, but kill people when they leave the temple. The more turmoil there is, the more prosperous the ghosts and gods are!

Pu Songling was good at talking about ghosts, and Wang Yuyang had a poem that said: [Let's talk nonsense and listen to it nonsense. Rain is like silk on the bean trellis and melon frame (Note: This is the realm of ghosts!). It is expected that you are tired of talking about human affairs and love to listen to ghosts singing poetry in autumn graves!] Perhaps he was not very happy living either, and seeing the ghost world might be better than the human world!

Qingming 234

— Daizi

I haven't been back to my war-torn hometown for several years. In this wicked city, as long as I am bored, the scenery of my hometown, with its bright flowers and dark willows, always unfolds in front of my eyes. Leaning against the green mountains with lush forests and bamboo, extending a green wheat field, following the wheat field, there is a stream of slowly flowing spring water with weeping willows on both banks. Here, you can often see some leisurely fishermen, squatting on the smooth rocks by the stream, basking in the sun and fishing. The buzzing of the yellow bees under the willow leaves is almost催人入睡(lulling people to sleep). Ah, that is such a peaceful village, such a quiet paradise!

In the past, during the Qingming Festival, when I and my younger brother followed my mother to visit the grave here, after kowtowing in front of my father's tombstone, we would run to the tenant's house. A group of familiar barefoot children would surround us, enthusiastically bringing tea and cigarettes, looking at the silk mandarin jackets on me and my brother with surprised eyes. When my brother and I made a fuss about going fishing, the children would happily抢着(scramble to) take the fishing rods and baskets. My mother was afraid that we would fall into the water, but the children's fathers all said [Don't be afraid, don't be afraid.] To reassure my mother, they even sent a young and strong man to protect us. I remember that the strong man patted his chest and said, [My name is Shui Sheng, water is no problem, I'm here!] We蜂子朝王似的(like bees swarming a queen) surrounded Shui Sheng and ran to the stream. When we caught a few fish, we thought we would have fresh fish to eat today. But as soon as we stepped into Shui Sheng's house, the table in the living room was already full of plates of big pieces of fish and meat, and they immediately urged my mother and us to sit at the upper seat. The fish caught today were for us to take to the city. Shui Sheng's eldest brother carried a风雨灯(storm lantern) on the way to see us off and said: [If you like fish, I will catch some more for you tomorrow.] We always brought some fish into the city every Qingming.

Later, we still went to visit the grave every year as usual. Our age increased, but荒芜(desolation) could be seen everywhere. The only thing left by the stream were the empty weeping willows. Shui Sheng and some strong men all said that they were [drafted] and never seen again. Our tenant was another person with the surname Wang. My mother said, [This old Wang is very hateful, don't look at his old age, he will play some tricks. If you don't pay enough rent, he will be evicted.] I felt that my mother had also changed. In the past, every time she came to visit the grave, she always happily told us some wonderful stories about the village, but now she didn't even put down her mind of calculating accounts for a moment. As soon as she walked to Lao Wang's door, my mother shouted about the rent problem, [You have to pay, we have to pay five years of food in one year!] My mother said with an iron face, and Lao Wang撲的(suddenly) knelt down. Lao Wang唠唠叨叨(chattered endlessly), and my mother唠唠叨叨(chattered endlessly) too. We had no food to eat that day, no fish to catch, we came into the city empty-handed, listening to my mother's complaints.

Later, I left my hometown, although the scenery of bright flowers and dark willows always unfolded in front of my eyes.

Rather than saying that I missed the quiet hometown, it would be better to say that the ruthless life of the city made me too uncomfortable. After several years of war, I actually made a big decision to go back. The city was already very desolate. Many of the once lively hotels and restaurants were closed. Although a few more red-light smoking houses had been added, there were very few people walking on the streets very early. As for my mother, she was lying next to her own opium lamp and looked even older. Whenever she mentioned the rent grain after the flood, she sighed and complained constantly. She had not dared to go to my father's tomb for a long time. But in order to hope that my father would bless us, my mother asked me to take advantage of the recent peace to visit the grave during this Qingming Festival.

The hometown scenery that I had often dreamed of was now realistically presented in front of my eyes again. The mountains were still lush with forests and bamboo, the water was still lined with weeping willows on both banks, but most of the fields were乱草(weeds), and people were looking at us with a pair of thief-like eyes. Hearing the sound of the wind in the treetops, it would make people suspect that something sinister was hidden in the阴森处(gloomy place), and one or two槛褛(shabby) men walking towards us with winking eyes would make people suspect that the coarse hand hidden under their clothes was摸着(feeling) a shiny steel knife. When my mother came today, she had originally decided to take this opportunity to find Lao Wang, but after kowtowing in front of my father's tombstone, my mother urged us to quickly pack up the offerings and go into the city before the sun set. At this time, if you stood in front of this tomb and looked at the森森(gloomy) mountains and streams, it really seemed as if a rough hand could reach out from anywhere. We couldn't help but毛发悚然(feeling our hair stand on end). My mother said with great regret [Shouldn't have come, shouldn't have come.] We entered the city today捏着一把汗(with our hearts in our throats). As soon as I entered the city, I took a deep breath; [Ah, hometown!]

Love Song of Rugao 235

— Hai Neng

(1)

Three or two pieces of bright red silk thread,

Woven into a ribbon to give to my lover;

Brother, don't dislike the ribbon being short,

Although the ribbon is short, the affection is deep.

(2)

Making friends with a girl across the field,

Coming to enjoy the cool every evening.

Patting the knees and sitting on the legs,

One person fans the wind, two people feel cool.

(3)

Making friends with a girl across the ditch,

The lover sends a headdress, but the girl does not accept it.

Not accepting the headdress is okay,

Don't think that others will abandon me.

Talking About "Red Hair" 236

— Mu Mutian

Opening Remy de Gourmont's [Le Livre des Masques], and flipping through it, you can see one cartoon after another by Vallotton. One of them may particularly attract your attention. It is a face drawn with a curve, with two small circles replacing the eyes. That is Jules Renard (1864-1910), the author of [Poil de Carotte].

Although looking back now, I feel that Renard is not such a great writer, around 1925, in the aura of symbolism surrounding me, Renard, Vildrac, and even the Catholic poet Claudel, all became my favorite writers. Renard's [Poil de Carotte] particularly pleased me.

Renard was a French local writer. Naturally, his works do not reflect the complex social life in Zola's [Les Rougon-Macquart]. However, in exposing the disharmonious points in the rural society at the end of the century, his work [Poil de Carotte] cannot be said to be without considerable significance. If we open the book [Poil de Carotte] and look at the cartoons drawn by Vallotton, we will all feel Renard's sarcasm and tears. In fact, I have not read the novel [Poil de Carotte] (1894) in detail. What I have read in detail is the one-act play [Poil de Carotte] that he adapted later. That gave me great satisfaction at the time. Renard can also be said to be a naturalist writer. In [Poil de Carotte], he accurately described the characters of his characters and their natural environment.

[Poil de Carotte] depicts the entanglement of a well-to-do landlord family in the countryside. A family of four, father, mother, elder son, and younger son. The father and mother are not on good terms. The father does not talk to the mother. Except for sometimes going to the city to file a lawsuit, the father goes out for hunting and other gentry-style pastimes. He is lonely. The mother is also lonely. The mother suffers from hysteria and often goes to the monk to pass the time. The book does not say whether she has any ambiguous points with the monk. If it is said that she is going to repent, but when she returns home, she tries her best to torture her youngest son. There seems to be a [unspeakable secret] between husband and wife. The mother loves the elder son. The father loves the younger son, but the mother dislikes him. She tries her best to manipulate her youngest son, and her son stubbornly and Confucianly argues with her. Although he is a boarding student in a middle school in the city, he has to go home for summer vacation. When he is at home, there is a play to be staged at home. On a summer afternoon, that one-act comedy is realized. I think this comedy of family disputes is quite meaningful.

However, although Renard pointed out that the family is a collection of people who do not understand each other, he has never been able to give a sociological explanation. His failure to understand society was naturally caused by the French social environment at the time. He can only passively negate it. He found a way out: to find comfort in [nature]. However, can nature really comfort unfortunate people?

A few years ago, when I was in Beiping, I translated the script of [Poil de Carotte]. At that time, the translation name was [Carrot Hair], which was published in the supplement of the North China Daily. Last year, Mr. Lin Qu also published a good translation of the novel [Carrot Whiskers] in [Free Talk]. Although it is not a great work, it is also very beneficial to translate it. But my idea is that for the sake of popularization, it is better to translate the title as [Red Hair], which is more concise. I don't know what Mr. Lin Qu thinks?

Renard has been dead for more than 20 years, and it is now the 70th anniversary of his birth. At this time, I hope that the novel [Carrot Whiskers] can be published as a single volume. However, the translator should add a critical preface. The Vallotton woodcuts are also best inserted.

Travelogue of Nankou (Part 2) 237

— He Jie

The next day was even more worthy of writing about: we were going to take a train to Juyongguan, which was more than ten minutes away. We got on the train at a station [whose name I unfortunately forgot again] and bought third-class tickets, but there was no room for another leg in the third-class carriage. A railway employee enthusiastically went to check the second-class carriage for us, but there was no empty seat either. He said generously:

[Then you can stand in this first and second class carriage, it's only a little more than ten minutes away.]

We had no choice but to listen to him. As each of us stepped up, the train moved forward.

Before we had stood firm, a military policeman of the 某团(certain regiment) in a grass-green woolen uniform suddenly popped up. He was short and always held his head up.

[Where are you from?].

He spoke Mandarin with a Hunan accent, using a voice like shouting slogans to soldiers. Before anyone could answer, he said the second sentence:

[You can't stand here.]

This time the voice was louder, full of a martial spirit.

[We're getting off at Juyongguan, it's not far.]

One of us said this.

[Don't you know, there are [important people] here!]

He said as if disaster was imminent. This was a bit strange. Everyone looked around at the same time, wanting to see how [important] the [important people] were.

But that military policeman [important people] shouted again　　 [Don't you know the stakes?]

When saying this, 威风(his majesty)　　　　, 好像(as if) we were all his enemies. 那时(At that time)　我倒想(I wanted to)　一　　,　　摄影家(photographer), 将那姿式照了下来(to take a picture of that pose), 倒也可以启发民族精神(It can also inspire national spirit).

Several people who knew the stakes advocated moving around, but there was really nowhere to go, so they had to stand in the area where the two carriages were connected. Afterwards, because we were standing outside the carriage, we had no way to see what happened. We don't know if that brave man was like　胜归来(returning in triumph), 经过凯旋门(passed through the Arc de Triomphe) with得意(complacency).

We suffered a bit, the carriage traveled through the mountain tunnel, and the coal smoke choked us so much that we dared not breathe.

Since this section has been written, the most exciting part is completed, and there is no need to continue writing. What can be added is that we actually returned to Beiping, none of us missing.

Observations on the New Life Movement 240

— Zhi

The call of the New Life Movement resounded like thunder. We read various declarations, speeches, and records about the New Life Movement in the newspaper every day. We felt that a kind of vigor had emerged in this　here country. Although it did not stimulate people's emotions like a storm, this peaceful and inspiring moral power, which leads people to a healthy and beautiful life, also has a great effect on the people who are unwilling to live in a careless manner.

Advocating a new life naturally negates the old life; what is the content of the old life? Perhaps it is necessary to say a few words about it here first.

First, in terms of the meaning of the times, the old life should refer to the life of the remaining feudal style and the life of capital plunder. For example, the lives of landlords, gentry, and unscrupulous merchants are all engaged in plundering other people's blood and sweat for a living, which is the so-called parasitic life. Secondly, in terms of the meaning of labor, there are many old remnants and young masters in China, as well as young masters from洋场(foreign concessions), who live a life of extravagance and desire without labor. Nowadays, there is also a kind of extortion life prevalent in society, that is, relying on a force to extort a group of weak people without power for a living.

There is also a large group of people in the old life who do not know how to live and are unable to live. They live a life of begging from door to door in荒村野店(remote villages) or街头巷尾(streets and alleys) every day.

The above is from the economic side, saying that the old life has so many meaningless contents. If we focus on the spiritual side, we can point out more and worse contents.

The first is that people's hearts are treacherous, and everything is讲求(particular about) using means: the second is laziness and vulgarity. This habit is almost a universal phenomenon in the so-called upper class,穿(dressing), 吃(eating), 喝(drinking) are readily available. The rich, big masters, or children of prominent families, and ladies who are装成(disguised) by money inherited from their ancestors or剥夺(seized) by themselves, these people are idle all day long, so they only smoke opium, play mahjong, play poker, watch movies, go to dance halls, dog tracks,回力球场(jai alai courts), gambling houses, or go to XX prostitutes, in order to消磨(while away) this life. Most of the middle class are also idle, do not want to work, and are perfunctory in their work. They would rather not work and sit at home in depression or go to seduce women. The lower class can't even talk about human life. Maybe it's not that they want to be lazy and vulgar, just because they have nothing to do, and they haven't climbed to the upper or middle class. These lazy and vulgar habits will make China's real social life more degenerate, and they are also cultivated by China's social environment.

The content of the old life is as corrupt as the above-mentioned尖儿尖儿的(pointed), so the advocacy of a new life is of course天经地义(right and proper), and no one should disagree. But what should be the content of the new life? In addition to the礼义廉耻(four cardinal principles of propriety, justice, integrity, and shame), 清洁(cleanliness), 朴俭(thrift), etc., which are suggested by the important people of the time, we feel that we need to supplement a few more points in depth.

That is, the New Life Movement should also pay attention to the actual lives of a group of people, reduce people's suffering from hunger and cold with the greatest effort, reduce the behavior of剥削(exploitation) in the world with severe sanctions, and implement labor life and eliminate parasitic life with effective methods.

To win a great achievement in this New Life Movement, it is not enough to rely solely on the call of leading figures. We should mobilize the power of the masses, pay attention to organized activities, and continue for a long time. Otherwise, it is also empty talk.

Layoffs 241

— Especially

Recently, a layer of gloom has clouded everyone's heart, and a kind of flustered expression floats on everyone's face.

No, it can't be said like that. This flustered expression is not floating on everyone's face uniformly. At least, most people are still showing a cheerful expression, as if they haven't realized that the unfortunate event of [layoffs] has happened. Those who realize it are only a small part of the majority!

Perhaps it's a kind of abnormal expression? After this news came out, work seemed to become more tense. The accumulated work slid by very quickly. This effect is rarely seen normally. In fact? Emptiness fills their hearts, being struck by a huge hammer, and what bursts out are sparks of emptiness that splash across their chests!

|| How is it? What news have you heard? ||

|| I wonder if this news is true?

Yes, people always ask this involuntarily when they reach a certain level of extreme tension and panic, even though afterward, they clearly know that the object of their inquiry is equally clueless.

The gloom has become heavier, heavier, so heavy that it blocks out even a breath of air. However, they still have to struggle, struggle, because only in struggle can there be a glimmer of hope.

In normal times, they always feel that time passes too quickly, and a day goes by in the blink of an eye. But now? They hate that it runs so slowly, neither dead nor alive, dragging on, adding more intense worry, annoyance, and boredom to everyone's body.

|| Well, get ready to roll up the bedding! Little Zhang said very seriously.

|| Huh? You: : : You, where: : : :?

Immediately, many people surrounded him, their eyes especially big, big, emitting flames, their faces piled with thick solemnity.

|| Where did you get the news?

|| Hmph, still don't believe it? Old Li saw it with his own eyes in XX office.

With suspicious hearts, the gathered people dispersed. They couldn't help but think to themselves:

|| Perhaps it won't be as many as he said? And, perhaps my name won't be among them? Hey, I've been here for six years! I haven't made any mistakes, and I haven't taken any leave. Maybe this will matter: : : : : :?

|| However, who dares to be so sure? If he insists on firing you, then, then: : : : Alas! There are still a wife, daughters, and mother at home, a burden of five or six people. My meager salary doesn't allow for any savings. What will happen then: : : :!

Their brains were dizzy, burning, almost exploding.

[Everything is destined. What's the use of thinking? Damn it, I don't have any connections. Let it be!] In the end, when there was no other choice, they could only shift all the responsibility onto [fate].

The event finally erupted one afternoon.

A notice was written in neat characters, so dark, so complete. Attached behind was a slip of paper. On that paper, each word was jumping incessantly.

This time, two section members, four clerks, and twelve employees!

Silently, the laid-off employees were organizing their belongings in their drawers, silently walking out of that gray,沉沉門, silently leaving a deep, bitter smile for the rest.

The next day, the office was quiet. The scene was very desolate. The energy of life had escaped. A layer of desolation struck deep into the hearts of those who remained.

Not many days later, the news came again:

|| It's not good. After the layoffs, the degree of contraction still doesn't match the budget. Now, the second batch is underway.

This was a bomb placed in front of their faces. For some reason, the previous panic was gone. All that could be seen was the even more severe sternness on everyone's face.

A Crude Psychoanalytic Study of Consanguineous Marriage 242

— Ling Bing

Yesterday, this publication carried an article by Mr. Lüsha on the issue of bloodlines being too close for marriage. This is an issue that Chinese people have always considered unproblematic. Just think about the deeply disgusted attitude that society takes towards love between young men and women of the same bloodline, and you can see how affirmative the word "unsuitable" already is. No matter how much the new figures who reject the cannibalistic nature of the old ethics and teachings, few dare to doubt the authority established by the old ethics and teachings on this matter. From this, we know that if all issues are not examined from a correct historical and scientific perspective, then the so-called work of destroying and expanding the clearing of the old ethics and teachings is nothing more than romantic momentum. Mr. Lüsha cited historical facts of consanguineous marriage and the prevalent marriage system in the Japanese imperial family as counter-evidence, which is very appropriate in his argument. According to the explanation of the American modern psychologist A.T. Reid, the terror of incest in human psychology and ethics has only developed relatively recently. In the ancient dynasties of Egypt and Peru, incest was practiced. Ancient Shintoism was also very lenient on this, and the authors of Genesis must have recognized the concept of incest as the only basis for explaining the descendants of Adam and Eve. Fraser said it well: [There is no law that encourages people to eat and drink, nor is there a law that prohibits people from being placed on fire. Because people drink and eat in the first place and do not burn their hands is due to instinct.] If people were naturally averse to incest, then there would be no need to legislate to force them to avoid it.

Toreton believes that the origin of incest is due to the fact that children of both sexes in the family have been together since childhood, so the first sexual desire that occurs naturally aims at the opposite sex who is close. As for the fact that all races have adopted strict legislation to ban it without prior agreement, that is because the elders of ancient tribes often monopolized the females and rejected the males, and were eventually killed by the joint efforts of the youths, and the youths each thought of monopolizing and rejecting the others, so they killed each other, so they agreed not to commit this offense to show prevention.

Mr. Lüsha believes that scholars criticize close relatives for marriage in order to prevent the double transmission of special genetic defects in the bloodline to their descendants. However, Toreton has a unique explanation for this: he believes that in the modern social system, the difficulty of bearing the burden of marriage makes the generally unhealthy elements tend to avoid difficulties and take the easy way out when it comes to the responsibility of marriage, and love between blood relatives often becomes a shortcut for such people to satisfy their desires. On the other hand, weak people do not have the confidence to compete in the social arena, so they choose people with close bloodlines (because close bloodlines have many conveniences in terms of approach) as their marriage partners, which is the general reason for consanguineous marriage. Since this kind of people are inherently endowed with deformity, it is only natural that their offspring are not strong. From this point of view, defects should be the cause and inheritance should be the proper result. Mr. Lüsha's view that inheritance is the cause and defects are the result is precisely a reversal of cause and effect.

The Mystery of Shanghai 243

— Zhi Cang

｜Two Strangers｜

In the southern goods department of S Company on Nanjing Road, there was a young customer who had just paid a dollar to have a piece of ham he had bought wrapped up by a shop assistant. Suddenly, he picked up the piece of ham, looked at it back and forth, and then put it down again. [I really don't know if this piece is good or not,] he said, as if soliciting the shop assistant's opinion.

[This piece of ham is not bad: : :,] A woman who was standing next to the young man, dressed like a young woman, was also buying something. Obviously, she didn't know the young man. Suddenly, she reached over and picked up the piece of ham and looked at it, saying to herself. This was not strange at all. Everyone was a customer.

[Thank you,] the young man turned around and nodded to her very humbly. His consciousness seemed to have gone beyond the scope of everyone being customers.

The ham had already been wrapped up and sent to the original counter by another shop assistant. The young man had to leave dejectedly. However, as soon as he turned around, he went to the foreign goods department and looked at this and that, and finally bought a tie.

The young man turned around and saw that the woman had already held a large bag of things under her arm and was walking towards him. The young man had been walking very slowly, but now he was dragging his feet on the ground, waiting for the woman to approach. [Are you free today? You bought so many things]. The young man's tone was flat and steady. The pace under his feet had already accelerated, matching the woman's, and they walked side by side.

The woman turned her head to look at him, but did not reply.

[It's quite heavy. Can I hold it for you?]

The woman seemed to smile, but still didn't say anything. The young man didn't wait for her second more obvious expression of consent, and his hands had already reached under her arm to replace the paper bag under his own arm. The two people walked, walked, even closer.

[Is there anything else you want to buy? Can we find a place to talk?] the young man asked.

[Why not? But I originally wanted to take a bath when I came out,] the woman said.

[Then, it's your treat, okay?] the young man said with a cheeky face.

[Why not?]

But the woman didn't mean to go out the door, but instead stepped into the elevator, so the young man had to follow in. At this time, the young man was really hesitant. He thought: [Can this really happen? Would she really treat? No way, no way! But I have nothing left but the two dimes I have left. What if: : : what do I do? And my family told me to buy this piece of ham and bring it back. I have to send it home today. Is it a trap? No way. Then, what should I do: : : Never mind, I'll see what happens to her in the end. Anyway, I only have two dimes on me.] The young man finally made an explorer-like decision.

The elevator stopped. They came out and walked to a hotel. Then, led by a waiter, they entered a quiet room. After filling out the circulation book, the woman took out a ten-dollar bill from her handbag, paid the waiter, and turned to the young man and said: [Do you need to eat something]? The answer was no. The waiter then retreated, and at the same time, the air in the room suddenly jumped up.

[Can you tell me your name?] the young man asked.

[Why are you so infatuated? I don't ask your name, and you don't have to ask mine, isn't that good?]

[Didn't you say you wanted to take a bath?]

[Now that I have you, I don't need it.]

Saying that, she sent a charming smile [Right?]

A drunken kiss melted their two hearts.

They satisfied their desires. It was late at night. When the two walked out of the company, the young man asked:

[When will we meet again?]

There was no answer. (End)

— Made by Chen Jingsheng

From then on, they became homeless dogs. The scouts reported that enemy reinforcements had arrived.

An Undeniable Answer 245

— Person

Five years ago, what great castles in the air floated in my mind, but after five years, five years later, today, besides the illusions before disillusionment, I dare not hope for anything anymore. I already know that Mr. What [school is a small society] is a lie. If school is really a small society, how can the first step I take into society make me tremble and shrink back and be at a loss what to do? [School is not a small society, but society is the real school.] This is the answer that two years of service have given me.

With the knowledge sold by teachers, I thought I was very full and rushed into society to make a living with good intentions. Therefore, in addition to being despised for my shallow knowledge and impracticality, I was unable to get enough to live on due to lack of qualifications. Therefore, I also know that qualifications are indispensable on the road to making a living. Oh! The current society has given us young people another kind of shackle. Qualification! On the road to making a living, you also need qualification as a backing!

For the sake of qualification, an unforgettable and cursed memory flashes into my mind. It was three years ago! I, that weak and pitiful me, had a burning desire to enter university, but to enter university, I had to have a high school diploma, so I stepped into school to get this so-called diploma, and on the other hand, give the desire for knowledge a chance to be satisfied. Trembling, I went to the school to register, and I was able to get the director of studies to agree and say: [Take the transfer certificate slowly, you can pay the fee and register for class first.] Things were decided like this. Except for paying the fee, there were no procedures, and I could move my bedding and luggage to school. I was full of enthusiasm and went to class with rapid steps, and then came back from class.

The classroom was so noisy that I couldn't believe it was a classroom. There were people singing, chewing peanuts, knitting velvet ropes, talking and laughing, sleeping, all kinds of strange things. Of course! What would the teacher ask the students to do? Only making trouble and fooling around are homework!

Each book is a thick, western-style, gold-lettered hardcover book. Inside, there are crab-shaped characters, as well as triangles! Sines! Vertical coordinates, horizontal coordinates: : : : : : I am really a little scared, but, strangely, at the same time, there is a slight heat in my heart because I think that this semester, I can get a lot of knowledge. But for a month, the book is still a brand new book. Later, I didn't even recognize our teacher's name. Because there were too few opportunities for our teachers and students to interact, the school authorities did not consider the needs of our students. For example, the task of using thoughts should be placed in the morning, but in fact, it was placed in the afternoon. Also, for example, the task of teaching six hours a week will be taught in two days｜three hours in a row each day. In this way, in terms of time, it is supplemented, but whether it is beneficial to students is a question that seems not very serious.

So, in school, you can eat, dress, sleep, fool around, spend money. You can ignore everything.

The school's dark secrets were exposed layer by layer, and my mysterious longing gradually faded. [Is school society?] I cannot deny the iron-like answer that two years of service have given me.

Starting with Venereal Diseases｜Discussion 3 247

Editor Sir:

After reading your publication's amateur mailbox yesterday, I am willing to contribute a little bit of my humble opinion to the readers, as a source of exploration, in order to achieve the goal of reducing the crisis of young people, based on the condition that your publication gathers ideas and benefits everyone.

Of course, [sexual desire is innate. It cannot be stopped,] so when young people reach a considerable age, after development is completed, they feel sexual boredom and the temptation of the opposite sex due to psychological and physiological impulses. This is the natural order. We should follow nature to find an object to make a reasonable marital union, as Mr. So-and-so said in his letter. Because economic conditions cannot be sufficient, he gives up the obligation to form a family. When the inner burning is strong, he uses the method of looking for flowers and asking willows to complete his dream of stealing jade and warming fragrance. This kind of behavior is nothing more than supporting the existence of the prostitution system, which will solidify the position of prostitutes in society. If the trend is spread, it will make the entire society fall into an unimaginable situation. Even the method of setting up a bureau to check and examine, which was proposed by Mr. So-and-so, is a wasteful attempt. In my opinion, in order to eliminate the urban evils of sexually transmitted diseases that are popular today, we should first correct the erroneous views before there is hope of a thorough clarification. If there are absurd people who indulge in Qin Lou Chu Guan because of the greed of carnal desire and the temptation of pornography, then the transmission of sexually transmitted diseases is not the fault of society but the self-inflicted misfortune of the patient. Moreover, the formation of society is the general term for the collection of individuals. If each young man and woman strictly promotes the formation of a rational family with one husband and one wife, prostitutes will naturally disappear and sexually transmitted diseases will naturally disappear. Reader Xing Su

Novel

Siamese Rhapsody (4) 249

— Yi Min

4. Bangkok

Bangkok is the capital of Siam. Because of the convenience of water and land transportation, Bangkok is not only the political center of Siam, but also the commercial hub of the entire country. When the ship enters the Chao Phraya River, we can see many strange buildings: some are like wooden pavilions, some are like terraces, some are like pigeon cages, and some are like castles. Different wooden houses are sparsely dotted along the Chao Phraya River. The most special thing is that those wooden houses are not built on land, but float on the river surface or are supported by wooden piles in the water. At the entrance of each wooden house, there is a small boat that is less than five feet long and can only accommodate one person. This is their means of transportation. Even children who are three or five years old can row small boats in the vast Chao Phraya River.

When the ship arrives at the dock, it is a different scene. There are lively roads and modern buildings. All the material civilization of the city is probably available here. If it were not for the extra-large rickshaws that can seat two people side by side, which make you feel unfamiliar, you would suspect that you have returned to Shantou or Shanghai, because not only the form of the shops is no different from the shops in Chinese cities, but also most of the clerks in the shops and the passers-by are our compatriots.

5. Strange Customs

Brothers and sisters can be husbands and wives

It is rare for brothers and sisters to marry each other in modern civilized countries, except for barbaric nations. However, this strange custom is still prevalent in the Siamese royal family. It is said that when the first king was plotting to usurp Zheng Zhao, his wife - Zheng Zhao's daughter - also participated in the secrets. Later, when he became king, he was afraid that his son-in-law would also follow suit, so he did not allow his grandsons to marry wives from outside. They could only marry their sisters. At the same time, if there was more than one princess, the rest would not be allowed to marry either, and would stay in the palace for life. From then on, the monarchs of Siam followed this practice without any doubt, even to this day.
